startled the Impresario ever since it has arrived. The scene shifts towards 
the wandering gambler:

  "A blackjack-playing, world-traveling, casino-dwelling free spirit..."

Here you will be given the chance to name the character, so name him Setzer 
and leave it at that. It appears that Setzer is the owner of the world's only 
airship. The party then decides to set up a meeting with Setzer. Now head 
south towards the Opera House.

=============================================================================
SETZER AND A NEAR COSTLY GAMBLE
Items: None
Party: Celes, Locke and whomever
Party's level: 13-16
=============================================================================

Inside the Opera House talk to the Impresario. He tells the party that Setzer 
might appear at the climax of scene 1 as he loves an entrance. That's when 
the party decides to grab him at that time, but that would cost the 
Impresario his job. He wants the play to be a success and does not want Maria 
to be abducted. Then the party decides that they will let Setzer grab Maria, 
but Celes will be the decoy since she looks so much like Maria and that 
should lead them to the airship. Celes however has some doubts because she is 
no Opera Singer, she then runs for the door and shuts it behind her. 

Inside however she practices, but doesn't sound so good as Locke has a laugh 
or two. However at the same time Ultros who is also in the Opera House wants 
to foil their plan by pretending to be Setzer. He lets the letter fly off to 
the party's direction but the party doesn't even notice it as they prepare 
for the play. D'haaaaa! Read it...! Then the scene moves over to the Opera 
play down below, and the Impresario plays out his role while depicting of a 
war between east and west. 

After the short play have Locke head for the dressing room to the right. In 
the dressing room talk to Maria um...I mean Celes. Locke seems too blushed to 
speak to Celes in proper English, but Celes still wonders why Locke had 
helped her back there. He did so because he once abandoned someone when she 
needed him. Afterwards have Celes check the score on the table, and try to 
remember the words, just skim through it, but if you have Ginkoba you'll be 
fine. After you are done head for the stage and the play will start. 

Also note that FFVII' Aeris theme most likely originated from Celes' Opera 
theme. Here you will have to select which part of the play comes next, mess 
up and you will have to start all over again. You will have to control Celes 
for a little bit in this play. Afterwards Celes is downstairs dancing with 
the prince as Locke looks over her.

  NOTE: In the U.S. version of Final Fantasy III, Celes had to remember
        more of the play instead of just selecting one part of the play.
        I think there was about three parts you had to make a decision in.
        Why was it only one decision in Final Fantasy VI? I just don't
        know.

Now leave back to the balcony, but before you do check the letter written by 
Ultros. It appears that we wants to ruin the Opera scene, so Locke better 
tell the impresario quick! The Impresario is startled but the play still goes 
on. Then the scene takes to the top of the play where Ultros has a weight 
ready to drop on Maria, I mean Celes! But it'll take him 5 minutes to drop 
it(odd, why would it take 5 minutes to drop a heavy object?), so that gives 
the party an indication of just how much time they have before they can save 
Celes. 

Talk to the man in the far right and he will help the two get up there. When 
you reach there hit the far right switch and then quickly head to the left 
side, and you will be at the top of the play. However before you can reach 
Ultros there are Vermin and Sewer Rats that will block your path so you will 
need to make the battles quick. 

  NOTE: On the SNES version you don't need to deal with load time like the
        PSX does. Even the load times after and before the battles including
        going through doors the time still runs! No kidding, everytime the
        PSX loads info onto the RAM you lose 2 seconds off the clock! So
        I'm just warning you that your time is much more limited on the PSX
        version than on the SNES version!

Don't worry if you lose the battles though, the Impresario will give you 
three more chances afterwards and all the events prior to Locke reading the 
letter from Ultros you will not have to go through again. When you reach 
Ultros he will push you over the top, when Locke brushes himself off he 
pretends to act along with the play, but oh, what bad acting! But a "lowborn 
thug" could never defeat Ultros(as said by Ultros)! Well since the Impresario 
has no choice he might as well make the most of it, "music!"
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
BOSS BATTLE: Ultros      HP: 2550
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
This battle will be tough, Ultros' Tentacle attack causes critical hits right 
from the start so you will have to keep your HP above 200, and heal 
immediately after he hits you with it. Use all of your powerful attacks 
against him like Dispatch, Aurabolt, Chainsaw, you know just like regular 
boss battles.

  NOTE: In the U.S. version of Final Fantasy III, Ultros splashes as he
        escapes, like if the stage was all water, however on the PSX version
        Ultros escapes regularly. Its odd!

After the battle Setzer finally reveals himself and takes Maria, Ce...Celes, 
that's it! However the Impresario is all giddy about the change in events. 
Afterwards Celes is put inside Setzer's casino room, but the other party 
members including Locke are already on board. Then when Setzer comes in he 
realizes that Maria is not Maria, and if she is not Maria then he does not 
want them onboard since she is not Maria. The party then try to sweet talk 
Setzer into helping them, Setzer sees what the party is getting at here but 
that does not mean that he is willing to help them. 

Now talk to Setzer, and it appears that the Empire has made him a rich man, 
but the party tells them about the cruel deeds of the Empire but Setzer never 
heard about this before. Setzer agrees to help the party if Celes becomes his 
wife, and as you can expect Locke is outraged. Celes however reluctantly 
agrees, but she wants to settle it with a coin toss as heads Setzer helps the 
party and tails she goes with Setzer, and a resounding acknowledgement is 
ajourned by Setzer. 

Celes then flips the coin and it lands on heads, so Celes wins! Setzer then 
picks up the coin and notices soemthing odd about the coin, it has identical 
sides! But Setzer admires that kind of low hustling and he will help the 
party with nothing to lose but his life. The party realize that they will 
have to land the airship a great distance away for obvious reasons and yes 
those graphics do look sweet right?

=============================================================================
THE TOWN OF ALBROOK AND THE SEIGING EMPIRE
Items: Elixir, Potion, Tincture, Warp Stone
Party: Whomever
Party's level: 13-16
=============================================================================

In this town and you will get a bit of information, and check the barrel to 
the far right of this town to the right of the inn to recieve a POTION. The 
town is filled with guards so going to the docks are impossible. Inside the 
pub is a clock, check it to recieve an ELIXIR, afterwards you can check the 
weapons and armor shop if you need anything, otherwise head out.

Vector should be up north, around to the top from where the airship is and
you will have to walk a LONG way. You can steal Tiger Masks from the enemies
that you encounter along the way though.

=============================================================================
TOWARDS VECTOR AND RESCUE OF THE ESPERS
Items: X-Potion, Flame Sabre, Zephyr Cape, Blizzard, Gold Armor, Dragoon
       Boots, Gold Helmet, Thunder Blade, Break Sword, Remedy, Tent
Party: Celes, Locke, and whomever
Party's level: 14-17
=============================================================================

In here buy any weapons and armor that you may need and then talk to the old 
man behind the crates in the center of this room. He will distract the guards 
while the party climbs the box and enters the facility. So when he does climb 
the boxes and around, when you reach behind the guards don't go near them 
otherwise a fight will ensue and you will have to start all over again. Now 
continue towards the top and into the heart of the facility. Do you hear the 
techno type of music? Pretty neat huh with it mixing with the clangs of 
metal. 

Continue towards the left side of the room and take the swinging hook over to 
the left side and also pick up the FLAME SABRE. Then head back to the middle 
of the room and through the pipes to pick up a TINCTURE. Then head for the 
pipe to the left and you will climb down to the lower part of the room. Pick 
up the X-POTION, and go towards the right to pick up the THUNDERBLADE and a
REMEDY. When your done head down to the bottom portion of the facility. At 
the bottom of the facility head towards the lower part of this room and you 
should find a TENT inside a treasure chest and a GOLD HELMET which is located 
at the bottom left of this room. 

Also don't forget to pick up the DRAGOONBOOTS relic at the left side and at 
the top left is a door which leads to a GOLD SHLD. When your done head for 
the walkrail where the Magitek armor is and it will take to the right side of 
the room, but then the party spots Kefka. He has drained the espers of their
powers and throws them to the walkrail that leads to the room below. Follow 
where the espers were thrown off. Here before you talk to the two espers take 
the room to the right and inside is a save point, so save your game and heal 
your wounds if any. When you talk to the espers they will attack you.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
BOSS BATTLE: Ifrit     HP: 3300
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
In this battle make sure that you are not equiped with the FLAME SABRE 
otherwise you will be healing Ifrit. Use Ice on him if you have it and 
hopefully someone did use the DRAGOONBOOTS relic so you can Jump Ifrit and 
also avoid some of his attacks at the same time. In this battle have Cyan use 
his level 4 SwdTech(if you have it, if not use the next best thing), have 
Sabin use his Suplex or Aurabolt, have Edgar attack with his Chain Saw, have 
Locke attack regularly(I suggest you give the DRAGOONBOOTS to Locke), have 
Celes use Ice magic on Ifrit and have Gau use any one of his Rage commands. 
After a while Ifrit will notice that you have Ramuh's powers and Shiva comes 
in and will sacrifice herself as well.

NOTE: Although there is some alternation between Shiva and Ifrit between
      battles, there were several occassional times when I had fought Shiva
      and Ifrit alone.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
BOSS BATTLE: Shiva     HP: 3000
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
I'm not sure if you are suppose to fight her, but if you do here are the
strategies. The game's Bonus menu lists her stats so I'm assuming that she is 
a boss, but I never really fought her before. This battle is basically the 
same as above except this time you will have to use Fire attacks obviously 
and equip the FLAME SABRE in this battle. After you defeat her Ifrit will 
come in and realize that you hold Ramuh's powers.

After the battle Ifrit and Shiva have little to live. Talk to the both of 
them and they will do the same thing Ramuh did with his power and entrust it 
into the party. So pick up the Magicite Shiva and Ifrit and continue onto the 
next room, the path Shiva was blocking. In here its just a long series of 
stairs, so make your way to the top. In this next room is the Magitek Res. 
Facility, to the bottom left of this room is a hidden passage which leads to 
a BREAK BLADE. After that continue onto the next room there will be a robot 
in your path. Talk to it and a fight will ensue.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
BOSS BATTLE: No. 024     HP: 4777     ITEM: Blizzard spear
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
This battle is fairly easy, he has no weaknesses even though he is a machine. 
Attack normally by having Celes attack regularly as with Locke. Have Cyan use 
his Swdtech, Sabin his Blitz, and Gau any of his Rage attacks. Have Edgar use 
his Chain Saw and continue this pattern while keeping your HP above 250.

After the battle continue through to the next room, here go up top and hit 
the switch. The espers doesn't have much long to live as they will 
turn themselves into Magicite. Then Cid comes in and examines the magicite 
and discovers something new about the espers. Then the magicite will break 
out and entrust their power in the party. It appears the Celes and Cid know
each other, and Cid thinks that Celes came here to cause an uprising.

Then Kefka makes his entrance and tells Celes to hand over the magicite 
shards, Locke is shocked to hear this as he thinks Celes has betrayed him. 
Celes however wants Locke to trust her, but he has doubts and then suddenly 
the Magitek troops come in and knock the party out as Celes clings on to the 
side. Celes now wants to protect Locke and maybe then he will believe her, 
she teleports the Magitek troops and Kefka away and she goes with them as 
well. 

Afterwards the contents of the capsules have spilled and the place is about 
to collapse, but he tells the party to quickly follow him. Cid realizes now 
that Kefka was using him and using the Empire and he decides to talk to the 
Emperor to have the war stopped. When you reach the bottom save your game and 
talk to Cid. Cid apparently was the one who raised her, but it was not his 
fault that Celes was forced to become a Magitek Knight and thus has done some 
inconsiderate things.

He feels bad for her and he wishes if he could talk to her and apologize for 
the way things have turned out. Then Kefka's laughter echoes through, Cid 
then pushes the party onto the mine cart and tells the party to escape. 
During the middle of this you will have to fight a couple of battles with 
MagRoaders. At the end of the trail you will encounter the boss of the 
railway.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
BOSS BATTLE: Number 128 & Left Blade & Right Blade     HP: 3278(#128) 
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
The Left Blade has 400 HP and the Right Blade has 700 HP. This battle will be 
pretty tough. Attach him constantly with the regular pattern of Cyan's 
Swdtech's, Sabin's Blitz, Gau's Rage, Edgar's Tools and Locke's regular 
attacks. Keep your HP above 280 for this battle and take out the Left Blade 
first and then the Right Blade and then the Number 128.

After the battle the party will crash into a Magitek armor and send both the 
cart and the armor flying! Here another save point opens up, so save your 
game and heal your wounds. Now head out of here and Setzer will meet up with 
you, the scene then shifts towards Kefka who is a bit angry about what just 
had happened. He sends mechanical arms to stop the party from leaving.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
BOSS BATTLE: Crane(2)     HP: 1800(Left Crane)  2300(Right Crane)
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
This boss will be very tough. Go through the regular routine like before but 
in this battle avoid using Fire magic as you will heal the cranes. Also keep 
your HP above 550, the Magnitude8 will cause a lot of damage to your party so 
you might want to watch out for that. Thunder spells work well to the right 
crane but the left crane is strong against that. Both however are weak 
against water attacks, but I don't think that you might even have a water 
spell at this point yet.

After the battle the party escapes from Vector and Locke is a bit worried
about Terra so they decide to head back to Zozo. Inside when the meet with
Terra, locke shows her the magicite. Terra then remembers her past, and it
appears that she was raised in an esper world. The scene flashes back
towards Terra's past, here you will control or reinact what happened. Have
the epser walk around and talk to the other espers and you will find 
someone laying on the ground, pick her up and Maduin(the esper you are
controlling) will take her to a bed for some rest. 

Then talk to the girl that you had saved and she will awaken. Maduin wants 
the girl to keep the pendant that protects the esper world, the espers are 
pretty upset about bringing a human back to health. Maduin however is tired 
of living in the human world, he sees the world as infectous, full of desire 
and greed. Then in the morning the girl had already headed for the gate, head 
for the gate atop. When you find Madonna she wants to leave because humans 
and espers can never co-exist, but how do they know unless they observe for 
themselves?

The two then have a baby, they've given the new born a name...Terra. Then its 
two years later and the troops are after magitek power. Emperor Gestahl wants 
all the espers and offers riches to any one who can capture an esper. 
Meanwhile Maduin and Madonna are looking over their child, then talk to the
Elder. The elder wants to cast a magical seal that will close off the 
humans from the esper world, but in his old state he might pass away, but 
he doesn't care just as long as the rest of the espers are safe. Madonna 
however wants to stay with Maduin. As you leave the esper thinks that it 
was the human's fault(Madonna) for causing all this trouble, but Maduin 
doesn't believe it.

Madonna then leaves and takes Terra to the gate so head for the gate, but the 
elder has already began casting the magical seal! When Maduin tries to head 
for Madonna troops and Emperor Gestahl block his path, but then the magical 
barrier starts it work and sucks out all the humans. Madonna is just ahead 
and as Maduin tries to pull back Madonna Terra is sucked out of the esper 
world and Madonna and Maduin go with her. Then Emperor Gestahl picks up Terra 
and discovers something, she's half human and half esper, Madonna wants 
Gestahl to take care of her, but Gestahl blinded by his ambitions wants to 
use Terra for greed and power purposes, Madonna tries to stop him but is 
knocked back. 

The scene shifts back to Terra and the magicite next to her is her father, 
she then realizes that she can control her power. It was also at the espense 
of an esper's life that Celes had acquired her powers. The party now heads 
back for Narche, and in the airship Setzer lets the party control the airship 
and gives you some instructions on how to use the air ship, you can also 
press start when you are on the airship to view the world map. Now heab back 
to Narche via the airship.

=============================================================================
THE RETURN TO NARCHE
Items: None
Party: Whomever
Party's level: 14-17
=============================================================================

Inside the party meets up with Banon and tells him about the way things went 
at Vector. Afterwards the party plans to combine Narche's money with Figaro's 
machinery to storm the Empire, but they are short on manpower. They think 
that if they can open the gate they can have the espers attack from the east 
and the party to attack from the North. But they must get the esper to 
understand and the only person that can do this is Terra. Terra's existence 
of half human and half esper is proof that espers and humans can exist. She 
then reluctantly agrees, then head for the airship. If you had not checked 
the clock inside the Old Man's house earlier for an ELIXIR you can do so now. 
Head for the airship and all of your party members are inside.

=============================================================================
GET THE ESPERS TO UNDERSTAND!
Items: Magicite(2), Ether(3), Assassin Daggar, Tempest Blade, Coin Toss 
       relic, X-Potion, Elixir, Tent, Atma Weapon, Genji Glove
Party: Terra and whomever
Party's level: 14-17
=============================================================================

When you are ont he airship have Terra be in your party. Then head for the 
east side of the southern continent and to the Imperial Base. Inside the 
party notices something odd, there are no imperial soldiers at this base. 
Then continue through to the right side and across the bridge and into a 
cave. In this cave there is a treasure chest that contains an ASSASSIN knife, 
pick it up and continue on. In this next room pick up the treasure chest 
which contains a TEMPEST blade for Cyan. Then continue on, and in this next 
room you will have to make your way across, but watch for the patterns in 
here, the bridge constantly shifts around, make a mistake and prepare to be 
damaged on the magma floor below you. 

Pick up the X-POTION and the COIN TOSS relic and continue onto the next room.
Here in Basement 3, pick up an ETHER and continue your way to the other side 
of the room. When you reach the first switch hit it and a bridge leading to a 
treasure chest will open, go to that treasure chest to pick up a GENJI GLOVE. 
Then continue on, when you see two switches hit the one on the left first and 
it will open a door and inside is a TENT and a save point, so save your game 
and heal your wounds. Then go back outside and hit the other switch outside 
and a Ninja will attack you. He's a pretty tough opponent because of the 
Water Edge attack that does about 270 HP of damage to every character. 

Defeat him as normal and after the battle he will tell you that he had 
somethign buried beneath the grand stairway. Then continue on and hit the 
next switch which will open up a staircase leading to a treasure chest which 
contains an ETHER and also to the next area. Continue onto the next area, 
there's some sort of hidden passage that you must walk through when you do, 
pick up an ELIXIR and continue on. Now you will see a couple of switches, 
don't hit them just yet, go to the bottom left switch and hit that one and it 
will reveal a doorway to another room that contains a MAGICITE(remember what 
I told you? this is not an Esper!), ETHER, ATMA WEAPON, and another MAGICITE. 

Now go back outside and there are two switches above you that I told you not
to hit, avoid hitting the right switch and go around it and check the 
treasure chest, it will ask you if you want to flip a switch, do not flip the 
switch. If you hit the two switches your path to the treasure chest will be 
cut off, but it doesn't matter, you can go ahead and hit those switches 
anyways. Continue on and pick up a MAGICITE and continue onto the next room 
and make your way to the Sealed Gate. When the party reaches the Sealed Gate 
the party will have to rely on Terra to convince the espers to side with the 
returners. Then suddenly Kefka comes in, its like he knew you were coming 
here all along! The party will have to keep Kefka busy while Terra slips 
through the gate. 

After the battle Terra opens the gate and all the espers come flying out of 
the gate and temporarily stunning the party and blowing Kefka away. Then 
after the gate closes back again it becomes blocked by the collapsing rocks 
and now head back to your airship by the door below in the next room, its a 
shortcut actually. When you reach towards the end of the Imperial Base the 
other party members will meet up with you and say that the espers went off 
west towards the capital, Vector. During the trip to Vector Terra notices 
something, the espers begin to fly in berserk fashion and then the airship 
goes out of control and crash lands and now head out of the airship and walk 
towards Vector.

=============================================================================
TOWARDS VECTOR AND AN UNEASY TRUCE
Items: Back Guard relic, Gale Hairpin, Revivify, Potion, Tincture
Party: Whomever
Party's level: 15-18
=============================================================================

********** Points Value **********

Below here is a chart, depending on which answers to take preceding to the
upcoming conversation will lead to a certain amount of points:

*** The Toast ***

To the Empire.                       2 points
To the Returners.                    1 point
To our hometowns.                    5 points

*** Kefka's Fate ****

Leave him in jail.                   5 points
Pardon him.                          1 point
Execute him.                         3 points

*** Apology for Doma ***

What's done is done.                 1 point
That was inexcusable.                5 points
Apologize again!!                    3 points

*** General Celes ***

Was she an Imperial Spy?             1 point
Celes is one of us!                  5 points
We trust Celes!                      3 points

*** Further Questions ***

Ask a question once.                 2 points
Repeat a question.                   -10 points for every question repeated

*** The Espers ***

Yes, the Espers have gone too far.   5 points
But you unleashed their power!!      2 points

*** Your first question ***

Answer correctly.                    5 points
Answer incorreclty.                  0 points

*** Care to rest? ***

Take a rest.                         5 points
Keep talking.                        0 points

**NOTE

*** What to say? ***

That all you really want is peace.   3 points
That you war's truly over.           5 points
That you're sorry...                 1 point

*** Will you accompnay Gestahl? ***

Yes                                  3 points
No                                   0 points

**********************

Essentially, once you have summed up enough points, a few things can happen:

0-39  points: South Figaro is liberated
40-49 points: Doma/South Figaro are liberated
50-59 points: Doma/South Figaro are liberated, stock room unlocked
60-69 points: South Figaro/Doma are liberated, stock room unlocked, 
              Tintinabar relic
70+   points: South Figaro/Doma are liberated, stock room unlocked,
              Tintinabar relic, Charm Bangle relic

**********************

**NOTE: Once you rest, you cannot carry over the conversation, and if you
        rest, you lose out on a potiential three extra points.

This will be a fairly long walk towards Vector since due to the fact that 
your airship is busted. When you reach Vector the whole place is burned and 
fire is still active. Make your way to the top of this place and it appears 
that the Emperor has been expecting the party. Talk to Emperor Gestahl and it 
appears that he has lost his will to fight, the espers came here to save 
their friends but when they heard that they had been perished the espers went 
berserk and decimated the town. The power of the espers was too great than 
what Gestahl had expected and now the espers must be stopped before the whole 
world is gone. 

There are still soldiers that prefer to keep on fighting, talk to as many 
soldiers as you can to make them understand. Along the way you can pick up a 
BACK GUARD relic, X-POTION, and a REVIVIFY. Try to talk to as many soldiers 
as you can before the four minutes is up, you will have to fight sometimes to 
get your point across as well. Afterwards the Emperor and the party are at 
the banquet and Cid is now a Returner. Here you will engage in a selective 
conversation choosing who you want to toast, what to do with Kefka, etc. The 
Empire has been leveled by the espers and Gestahl has finally come to his 
senses and realize that the espers must be stopped otherwise there will be no 
world to live in. 

The Emperor will head towards Cresent Island where the espers are and he asks 
if you want to accompany him, if you choose yes General Leo will go along as 
well, if you choose no the party will make it across their own way. 
Afterwards Locke will go with Terra, but he smells a rat, the party just 
can't trust the Emperor like that. The rest of the party will stay at Vector 
to investigate things. Now head out and south towards Albrook.

=============================================================================
ALBROOK AND THE TRIP TO CRESENT ISLAND
Items: None
Party: Whomever
Party's level: 15-18
=============================================================================

When you reach Albrook head for the docks to the south part of town. Talk to 
General Leo and he will tell you that he has acquired Celes and has hired 
Shadow to help the party. Locke is surprised to see Celes and when he tries 
to talk to her, she runs away. General Leo tells the party to get some rest 
so go to the inn  and get some rest. In the middle of the night Locke heads 
out of the inn and finds Celes, he tries to talk to her but she still remains 
silent and runs off. In the morning head for the docks and talk to General 
Leo, during the middle of the voyage Terra and General Leo have a talk. 

Terra thinks its a bit funny that the Empire once manipulated her and now she 
is working with the empire, but General Leo reminds her that not everybody is 
like Kefka. General Leo knew Terra was being used as a biological weapon and 
he did nothing about it and he feels that he is no different than Kefka. 
Terra still feels she lacks of something...love. General Leo understands, but 
Terra is just young. She wants to know what love is now. Shadow then comes 
out, he decides to sleep under the stars and overhears their conversation, 
but he had no intention to. She tries to ask Shadow for help, but he tells 
her that she must look within to find her answers. Then Locke comes out, and
he has a high sense of sea sickness. Talk to General Leo and Locke, then when 
Locke leaves Celes wants to talk to him, but Locke ignores her and leaves. 
Now when you are ashore head northeast towards the town of Thamasa.

=============================================================================
THAMASA AND A SHOCKING SURPRISE
Items: Ice Rod, Echo Screen, Fire Rod, Green Cherry, Phoenix Down, Soft,
       Eyedrop
Party: Whomever
Party's level: 15-18
=============================================================================

The party finds a mother nursing her child, she says "Cure" but then sees the 
party and quickly looks for her "Cure Medecine" but the child wants her 
mother to use Cure on her, what are they talking about? Now head inside to 
the top right house and talk to the old man inside:

  "An elderly gentleman, pure of heart, and learned in the way of 
   monsters..."

Now enter his mae in as Strago and leave it at that. The party then asks him 
about espers, but he's not really familiar with the word. However he 
hesitantly denies it, but the party spots that and the music shifts as a 
young girl comes in.

  "In her pictures she captures everything: forests, water, light... the very
   essence of life..."

Now name her Relm so you can follow the walkthrough better. She then asks who 
the people are and if they can use magic as well, but Strago tells her to 
keep it down. She then sees Shadow's dog, but Shadow warns her that he bites. 
Strago tells her to go to her room, but Shadow's dog follows her. The party 
senses something a bit odd and decides to take a look around. Now take a rest 
in the inn, and the innkeeper who usually charges 1500 GP for a night's stay 
for strangers now will let you sleep in his inn for 1 GP. Then later in the 
middle of the night Strago wakes the party as Relm is trapped in the 
neighbor's house and a fire has broken out. 

He asks the party to help and Shadow is a bit slow to acknowledge. Now head 
for the house below Strago's house and a fire has gone rampant. Strago then 
casts an Ice spell, but the Mayor comes in and tells him that magic is 
forbidden, but Strago doesn't care, and the Mayor seems like he has no 
choice. The people in this town gather to try to put the flames out by magic 
but are unsuccessful in doing so. Then Strago and the party decides to go in, 
but you will have to avoid the flames. IF you do encounter a Flame a battle 
with three Ballons will start. Make your way towards the center of the house, 
along the way you can pick up an ICE ROD and a FIRE ROD. When you reach the 
center top of the house the FlameEater will attack you.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
BOSS BATTLE: FlameEater      HP: 8400
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
In this battle have Strago use his AquaRake, have Locke attacks as normal and 
if Terra has an Ice or Ice2 spell then use it. The FlameEater will call for 
about 4 Balloons to join the battle as well which obviously makes the battle 
a lot tougher. Keeo your HP above 100 and continue the same pattern until 
he's gone.

After the battle Interceptor finds Relm unconsious, then the flames in the 
house knock the party out, and then they begin to gang up on Interceptor, but 
Shadow comes in and takes out the flames and uses a Smoke Bomb to get the 
party out. Then they find themselves in Strago's house, who tells them that 
this is the Village of the Mage Warriors. It was long ago that humans used 
magicite to gain magical powers, and later they became known as Mage 
Warriors. It was after the War of the Magi that the espers fled to the other 
realm and left the Mage Warriors to defend for themselves. 

The humans blamed the Mage Warriors for causing the war and they were hunt 
down like animals. A few Mage Warriors escaped and found refuge here, their 
powers have weakened over time. The party needs Strago's help and he is 
willing to do so for the party saving Relm. Relm wants to come along but 
Strago won't allow her to do so. So if the espers are in the world where are 
they? Their in the mountains to the west, mainly because the mountains have 
strong magical properties. Legend has it that the espers were created there 
so the party decides to have a look. So exit out of the house and you will 
see Shadow(who left earlier) outside. Shadow wants to search for the espers 
his own way. So now that he is out of your party head west towards the 
mountains.

=============================================================================
A FATE UNDENIED
Items: X-Potion, Chocobo Suit, Tabby Suit, Heal Rod
Party: Whomever
Party's level: 16-19
=============================================================================

In the mountains head inside and pick up a HEAL ROD and head towards the top 
right of the cave, and yes that is Relm following you, but the party does not 
notice it. Then continue on and when you reach a room with three gold statues 
in the middle head for them. It appears that the three statues created magic 
as we know it and they are the source of all magic. It is said that the 
espers made these images and arranged them in a special place as the statues 
represent power beyond comprehension. It appears that the other magic flashes 
are hidden beyond human reach, most likely beyond the gate. Afterwards head 
for the left side of the room but before the party can do that they are 
attacked by Ultros and he mentions Ziegfried, wait a minute. That bozo from 
the Phantom Train? Then he will attack you as it seems that he has not 
learned his lesson yet.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
BOSS BATTLE: Ultros     HP: 22000
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
This battle isn't so tough. Watch for his Tentacle attack, it will deal about 
100 HP of damage to every character when he spreads it so keep your HP above 
200 just to be safe. Attack like normal but since Ultros is an Octopus don't 
attack him with Strago's AquaRake, otherwise you will heal him. After losing 
a certain amount of HP Relm will come in(Relm's music sure is pleasant on a 
hard day's work, especially to relieve stress wouldn't you agree?). She will 
then talk to Ultros, Ultros will seem a bit angered by her as all she wants 
is just a portrait of the octapus. She then starts to get a bit down and is 
about to jump down, Terra stops her before she does and whispers something in 
Terra's ear. Terra then yells at Ultros for being such a bother to Relm, and 
Locke and Terra finally convince Ultros to tell Relm to draw Ultros a 
portrait. Ultros then casts Haste and Safe on himself, and no this is not for 
the battle but to make himself look a bit better for the portrait(!). Have 
Relm use her Sketch command and Ultros can't believe that he is no more than 
just a mere ocatpus. Then Ultros escapes.

After the battle Relm is excited that she had helped out the party so much 
and the party reluctantly lets her join. Then continue onto the next room and 
there are three switches on the floor. Now take the bottom left switch and 
then you will be dropped to the floor below. Later you will make your way 
around until you find the espers, and it appears that they are out numbered. 
Relm and Strago try to escape but are but off by the other espers. Yura then 
tells the other espers to stop and Terra confronts him, but Strago senses 
very high magical powers from Terra that it frightens him. 

Then afterwards Yura senses something in Terra and that he senses some 
familiar powers in her. The espers had set up a rule that they were not 
allowed through the gate and they had to fly through the gate to save the 
other espers that had been kidnapped. The espers had lost control of their 
powers when they had fled through the gate and leveled an entire city and 
innocent lives were lost. Locke wants the espers to come with them to talk 
peace to the Emperor in Thamasa. Later the scene shifts towards Thamasa and 
General Leo and and Yura talk things out. 

Yura apologizes for his actions, but he feels that an apology does not excuse 
them from their actions, but General Leo thinks it is the humans who have to 
apologize because they were so power hungry. Then when all is said and done, 
the party and espers laugh about it, but as does Kefka. He comes in with 
Magitek soldiers as they blast the party and General Leo's soldiers. It 
appears that Kefka is acting under the Emperor's orders to bring back the 
magicite remains to the Emperor. He then turns the espers into magicite as he 
wants the town destroy as well. After Kefka sends one of his troops to knock 
out General Leo, he awakens. Don't try to leave town though because Guardians 
will block your path and if you do lose you will have to start over again. 
Now talk to Kefka and a a fight will start.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
BOSS BATTLE: Kefka     HP: 5000
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
In this battle have General Leo FIGHT, he has the relic that allows him to 
use X-Fight. But if you want you can use SHOCK, which looks awesome! After
defeating Kefka he hides himself, and then Kefka calles for Emperor Gestahl. 
He apologizes to General Leo for decieving him as all he wanted was power, 
but then suddenly he changes to Kefka as it was him all along. General Leo 
was only fighting Kefka's shadow during the battle and after words Kefka 
sends General Leo a fatal wound that kills him.

After the battle a wave of energy flood the town and the scene shifts towards 
the Sealed Gate as the espers come flying through the portal as they try to 
help their fallen friends as they fly towards Thamasa. He then completely 
harnesses the power of the other espers as even another esper who challenges 
him but even he falls to Kefka's powers. Then he captures the rest of the 
espers' powers as things don't look good. Later when Kefka leaves the party 
mourns over the death of General Leo, all people seem to want is power. 

Then Interceptor comes in and is badly wounded as it appears that Shadow is 
gone as well. The party is worried about Edgar and the others and Terra wish 
she could say that they were safe, but then the other party members come by 
and meet up with the party. It appears that they've been had, the Emperor was 
a liar all along. Edgar had gotten to know a girl who had brought them tea 
who later blurted out the entire plan. The other party is shocked to hear 
that General Leo was killed as he was their finest soldier. The party then
decides to think up of a new strategy as Relm wishes to come along, but
Strago insists until Relm forcefully sways Strago's decision. The party then 
heads for the airship to discuss their plans.

=============================================================================
FLOATING CONTINENT AND FLOATING MISERY
Items: Murasame, Elixir, Beret, Atma Weapon(steal from Atma Weapon), Hardened
       knife
Party: Whomever
Party's level: 17-20
=============================================================================

On the airship it appears that the Empire is headed for the statues. The
scene then shifts towards Kefka and Emperor Gestahl and they appear to be at 
the brink of obtaining the espers. Terra senses that the world is in groaning 
pain as suddenly the land rips apart taking with it innocent lives as a giant 
continent is floated upon the world. Kefka and Gestahl are laughing about it, 
but the party seems worried. The statues were sealed away a long time ago, 
but if the statues are ever moved out of alignment even an inch the resulting 
imbalance of power would result in the entire rearrangement of the planet. 

Now head for the floating continent if you want, but if you need time to 
prepare then head down to the shops and buy some extra items. When you are 
all done head head for the floating continent but you will need to devise a 
party of 1-3, you can't have four in your party, why? You'll see soon enough. 
But before you can get on the floating continent the IAF or Imperial Air 
Force is here to stop you and you will have quite a bit of work on your 
hands. After a few battles with the Sky Armor and Spit Fire(s) you will 
eventually meet up with Ultros.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
BOSS BATTLE: Ultros & Chupon     HP: 17,000(Ultros) 10,000(Chupon)
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
Don't be shocked by the HP, you only have to lose them about a few thousand
hit points, after you damage Ultros enough he will call for his friend 
Chupon.(For those of you wondering Ultros and Chupon does not work for the 
Empire) This is also the first time you fight Ultros in the too hip boss
music. Keep using all of your best attacks and such and keep pounding him.
Lose Ultros about 4500 and his friend Chupon will come. After losing
Ultros about 8000 HP the second time you will finally defeat him and you
will have to lose Chupon about 10,000 to defeat him. When you defeat
Chupon he will use his Sneeze attack which will blow everyone away from 
battle.
 
After the battle the party is blown off the airship and another boss
approaches them. Note that even though you were severely wounded the last
battle you come to the next boss battle fully healed up.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
BOSS BATTLE: MissleBay & Laser Gun & Air Force & Speck    HP: 14,720(total)
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
This boss will be tough, watch for your HP and keep them above 280. First
take out the Laser Gun and MissleBay so you won't have to deal with them. 
Then concentrate your attacks full force on the Air Force. After destroying
the MissleBay and Laser Gun the Air Force will release a Speck which will
absorb all magic(including Ultima in which I used the Gameshark to get at
this point in the game!). Hit it with a physical attack and it should be
gone, but if you don't get rid of it quick you will have trouble damaging
the Air Force with magic. Also at this time it will begin a countdown
starting from 6, if you do not destroy both the Speck and AirForce you
will be eating the WaveCannon, a powerful attack(that has some cool special 
effects!) that does anywhere from 500-640 HP of damage to every character in 
your party! That's what makes this boss so hard! After defeating the boss you 
will acquire the CZARINA RING.

NOTE: When you encounter Gigantos, you can use the Phantom Esper to dodge
      his attacks.

You will now be on the Floating Continent, talk to Shadow and he will join 
your party and it appears that the Empire tried to kill Shadow when they had 
obtained the statues. After obtaining Shadow and saving your game head right 
and towards the bottom, the path should open up automatically, then check the 
blue orb just ahead to pick up the MURASAME blade for Cyan, then continue on 
towards the right and the path will open up for you(don't head for the stairs 
just yet) and it will lead to another blue orb and a monster will attack you, 
but its a VERY tough monster. 

Use all your best attacks and throw anything you may have at him, his Throat 
Jab attack does over 500 HP of damage so you must watch out for that. After 
the battle you will recieve a HARDENED knife. Heal your wounds also and then 
continue onto the top, it will take you to the bottom path of the floating 
Continent. Then head down and hit the switch and it will open up the right 
side for you, then continue on and go to the next transporter. Here you will 
see two other transporters so take the one on the left, it will take you to a 
switch at the bottom.

Hit that switch and the path below will pave way for you, then continue on to 
the top left and hit that switch as well and make your way down and around. 
Keep going right and you will see a switch, don't hit it just yet until you 
have picked up the blue orb and it will give you a BERET. Then head for the 
bottom transporter and it will lead to a save point, so save your game and 
heal your wounds. Then continue on back and hit the switch at the top left 
and it will open up a transporter.

Go to it and you will end up on the heart of the Floating Continent, and
you will also have the chance to head back to your airship, if you choose
to go back to your airship you will head back to your airship but you will 
have to go through the entire Floating Continent all over again. Choose no, 
unless you really have to go back for some needed supplies, and head towards 
the center and talk to the monster guarding your way and a tough fight will 
ensue.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
BOSS FIGHT: AtmaWeapon      HP: 24,000
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

NOTE: Another highly useful tip from Earthq:

  "Atma Weapon (on the Floating Continent) can be defeated a LOT more easily 
  if you obtained Osmose and Rasp from Magicite Shiva.  When you wear down 
  his magic points to zero, he's done for (because remember he said he was 
  pure energy?)"

In this battle it will be very tough, use all of your best attacks and have 
Edgar use his Drill attack. You can also steal another ATMAWEAPON from this 
guy, do so if you like but you must have Locke in your party. Keep attacking 
him with your strongest attacks and keep your HP above 450, yes that's right. 
He will use Flare at some point, and most likely your party member will not 
survive that. But definitely watch for the Quake attack that does about 600 
HP of damage to every character.
 
After the battle Shadow has sold his rights to the Empire and cannot fight
with you so he leaves. Then the party approaches Kefka and Gestahl, but Celes 
also comes in as well, but it appears that the party is too late. Gestahl has 
already taken in some of the statues' power, Celes tries to convince him tos 
top but Gestahl shows the party is awesome power, and every party member but 
Celes is stunned. Gestahl wants Celes to rule the world with him, Kekfa tells 
Celes if she kills the party members her past treachery to the Empire will be 
forgotten. 

She takes the sword and thinks about the situation, would she really betray 
her friends? No, power only breeds war as she turns around and stabs Kefka. 
He really HATES Celes for doing that as he flops dead on the ground, but he 
doesn't die as he uses the power of the Statues to revive himself. But if 
Kefka tries to revive those statues it will destroy the world that they are 
trying to possess, but Kefka doesn't listen as Kefka and Gestahl enter
battle against each other. Gestahl doesn't want Kefka to do so as he tries to 
put Kefka into a deep sleep, but Kefka laughs. 

Gestahl uses Fire3 and Flare but nothing happens as Kefka is unharmed due to 
the fact that Kefka is in the field of the statues. He then commands the 
statues to attack Gestahl, it misses and sends the two flying back. After a 
few tries Gestahl is finally hit and Kefka pushes Gestahl off the Floating 
Continent down to the Earth below. Kefka then rearranges the statues, but 
Shadow then comes in and pushes the statues back into place and the rest of 
the party are now free. 

Shadow tells the party to run but he can't stop the chain reaction, but he 
guarantees the party that he will meet up with them again. You will have 6 
minutes to escape, and along the way you will have to fight against several 
Naughty(s) and a Nepura at the end of the path. Its a bit tricky picking up 
that Blue orb, try to go around without going near the blue orb and pick it 
up to recieve an ELIXIR. When you arrive at your destination you will have 
the option of JUMP or WAIT, choose WAIT and Shadow should come by and meet 
with you when your time reaches under 10 seconds. 

After the party lands on the airship the statues begin to unleash its 
incredible energy as it levels the land below. The party tries to escape the 
statues' power but the power is too great as it splits the airship in half 
and sends the party members flying across the world. Afterwards a giant and 
very impressive Napalm like explosion emits from the field as the world is 
changed forever.

=============================================================================
=============================End of World of Balance=========================
=============================================================================

=============================================================================
A WORLD FOREVER CHANGED
Items: None
Party: Celes
Party's level: 19
=============================================================================

Here you will awaken as Cid has tended to Celes for over a year since the
statues' corruption. It appears that they have landed on a tiny deserted
island with a few strangers, but it appears that they have died of boredom
and despair. Cid doesn't even know where Locke is or if he even is alive
at all, Celes thinks that the entire party might have been wiped out as
the world continued to slide into ruin from that day one year ago. 

Cid however has not eaten in days ever since he became ill, but he doesn't
want to eat fish but its the only thing to eat here! While Cid lies down 
go look for a fish for him to eat outside, he will live longer if you catch 
him a fast fish, but since he is suppose to die anyways it really does not 
matter. Keep doing this until he starts to cough and he wants to thank you, 
after that go outside and pick up another fish and walk back inside to Cid. 

This time he does not respond, she keeps trying to get Cid to eat, but its 
too late. Celes can't even believe that Cid is gone and she decides to take a 
walk up along shore, she then finds a small letter on the floor, when the 
other people where feeling down they use to jump off the cliff up 
north...perked 'em right up! She feels alone that every one is gone, even 
Locke, the one who promised to protect her. She jumps off the cliff just to 
see her friends on the other side. Then she washes up shore in front of Cid's 
house, a bird wakes Celes back up, but she gets a bit angry that the bird 
nursed her back to health(figuratively of course) and then notices a bandana, 
could it be that Locke is still alive? Celes believes so, now head back to 
Cid's house. 

Inside you will find a letter next to Cid, check it and he will tell you that 
her friends are still waiting for her and that the stairs next to the stove 
awaits her road to freedom. So go check the staircase next to the stove to 
the left and you will find a small hidden room containing a raft, she says 
her last goodbyes and leaves off. LAter you will end up near a town, enter it 
and try to gather some information.

=============================================================================
THE RETURN TO RUINED ALBROOK
Items: None
Party: Celes
Party's level: 19
=============================================================================

In here talk to the town people and get some information. You will hear about 
talk of the 8 dragons and some Crusader power and also a man who was 
searching for his friends who went up north to Tzen. So go there and you 
might want to buy some new weapons and armors and relics if you do need them.

=============================================================================
THE RETURN OF SABIN
Items: Pearl Rod, Drainer Sword, Hyper Wrist relic, Magicite, Tincture, Heal
       Rod
Party: Celes
Party's level: 19
=============================================================================

When you enter this town suddenly a loud crash can be heard, head for the
center of town and you will find Sabin lifting up an entire house! But Sabin 
can't move otherwise the house will collapse and Celes must save the children 
inside. Inside there is a HEAL ROD, PEARL ROD, HYPER WRIST, Monster-in-a-box, 
TINCTURE, MAGICITE, another Monster-in-a-box, and a DRAINER sword. Inside 
there will be some random encounters, quickly head for the boy inside the 
house first and get him out, you will be given a rather lengthy 6 minutes to 
do so. 

Afterwards the people dive for cover as the house collapses as Sabin jumps 
away. Celes is shocked to find Sabin, as she had given up hope, but now that 
she has found Sabin they may all be alive! Now they must search for the other 
party members. Now head for the northeast part of town and you will find a 
man hidden behind some trees, he's not exactly super visible, but he is 
spotable. Talk to him and he will give you a stone for 10 GP, do so and you 
will recieve the Magicite Sraphim. Afterwards head east out of town to 
Mobliz.

=============================================================================
THE TOWN OF MOBLIZ AND THE LOSS FAITH OF TERRA
Items: None
Party: Celes, Sabin
Party's level: 18-20
=============================================================================

Head towards Mobliz to the far east, its a rather long walk through a bridge 
though. Inside when you walk in two dogs will block your path and a small kid 
will come out, he will then go back in and hide. Go to the house in which he 
went inside and go downstairs and the party will finally meet up with Terra 
for the first time since the incident over a year ago. She's happy to see the 
party, but when they talk about going to stop Kefka Terra walks away. Follow 
her and talk to her, she will tell you that she can fight no longer. 

After the day the world changed Kefka directed a beam towards the town and 
all the adults of the town died while protecting their young. Terra felt that 
the children needed Terra and she can't leave them, Duane then comes in and 
tells the party that they can't take her away. Terra can't fight because she 
lost her will to fight because the kids made her feel something that she had 
never felt before. Now leave, as the party leaves a kid informs Terra that
Phunbaba is coming, Terra then goes out to confront Phunbaba as he is an
ancient demon that was released when the world came asunder.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
BOSS BATTLE: Phunbaba      HP: 28,000
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
This battle Terra has no hope of winning, so just lose because all of your 
attacks will do jack.

After the battle Celes and Sabin come back, but then Phunbaba attacks them as 
well, time to teach this guy a lesson.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
BOSS BATTLE: Phunbaba      HP: 28,000
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
Here in this battle have Sabin perform one of his Blitz and have Celes attack 
regularly and keeping the party's HP up above 300. Keep this same pattern 
going until he escapes.

After the battle Terra is injured but otherwise fine and recovering quickly 
as she has lost her fighting edge as well as her fighting spirit. Terra 
decides to stay in Mobliz as she cannot be of any further help to the party. 
The party then leaves, but the kid stops you and thanks you for stopping 
Phunbaba and during his hastily retreat he had dropped the magicite Fenrir. 
Afterwards head northwest outside of Mobliz to find the town of Nikeah.

=============================================================================
THE TOWN OF NIKEAH AND GERAD
Items: None
Party: Sabin, Celes
Party's level: 18-21
=============================================================================

When you reach the town of Nikeah head for the pub, inside talk to all of the 
thieves and he will leave. Now leave outside the pub and head to the trade 
area in the center of town and talk to the guy who looks like Edgar. Talk to 
him and he will deny that he Edgar(could it be possible that he has 
amnesia?), as he trys to avoid you keep talking to him. He calls Celes "my 
lady" and she knows Edgar would only say "my lady" and Gerad is a bit 
shocked, but he tells her that "my lady" is used all over the world. Then 
follow him towards the docks, the party will conceal themselves from Gerad's 
view as they overhear the conversation. The party then sneaks onto the ship 
as it heads towards South Figaro. 

=============================================================================
RETURN TO SOUTH FIGARO
Items: None
Party: Celes, Sabin
Party's levl: 19-21
=============================================================================

In this town when you arrive head to the mansion on the north part of town 
and enter through the draft room and make your way around until the area with 
the numrous staircases and the path earlier that was blocked, you can now go 
through to basement 2 to pick up an X-POTION and an ETHER. Then head for the 
inn and talk to Gerad, he still denies the fact that he is Edgar, but why? 
Then head out and go towards west out of town to the South Figaro cave.

=============================================================================
FIGARO VIA SOUTH FIGARO CAVE
Items: Soul Sabre, Crystal Helmet, X-Potion, Ether, Gravity Rod, Regal Crown
Party: Celes, Sabin
Party's level: 19-21
=============================================================================

Inside Ziegfried will be in your way, talk to him and it appears that he will 
check inside for monsters and tells you to wait, but don't bother, just head 
inside and make your way through until you see Gerad and the theives. They 
will feed the turtle something and the little turtle will create a stepping 
stone for the theives and Gerad and Ziegfried will be right behind them. 
Follow the theives and Gerad through and you will notice that all the 
treasure chests are gone, thanks to the thieves.

In the next room Ziegfried will take the other treasure chest, follow him to 
the next area and you will now be inside Figaro castle. Continue through 
towards the engine room and make your way around and make sure you pick up 
the CRYSTAL HELM, GRAVITY ROD, X-POTION, and an ETHER. Then make your way 
through to the top left door and pick up the REGAL CROWN. Then head back and 
make your way to the center of the engine room, the party sees the thieves 
and Gerad and also the cause of the problem with Figaro castle. Gerad then 
tells the thieves to get the treasure while he takes care of the creature 
that has been a problem for Figaro Castle. Gerad finally admits to the party 
that he is Edgar, so aren't they going to give him a hand?
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
BOSS BATTLE: Tentacle(4)     7,000(1), 5,000(2), 4,000(3 & 4)
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
This battle will be tough, have Edgar use his CrossBow, Celes her Ice magic, 
and Sabin use his AirBlade blitz, if he has it, otherwise just have him use 
pummel. They will occasionally use Sieze, and it will capture a party member, 
so any damage done to the tentacle the party member will feel a fraction of 
it, but don't let that stop you from destroyng the boss though.

After the battle Edgar tells why he did not wanted to be known as Edgar
because he wanted to use the thieves that had escaped and they lead them to 
their secret cave. Then Edgar hears the thieves coming and hides, the thieves 
leave as they thought Gerad was swallowed up by the monster and Edgar's 
intention was never to get the treasure anyways. Now go into the treasure 
room and you will see that all the treasure chests have been checked and 
emptied, but check the center statue to reveal a SOUL SABRE. Now return to 
the top floor of the engine room and the driver will lift the castle to the 
surface. Now talk to the driver again and head towards Kohlingen.

=============================================================================
RETURN TO KOHLINGEN
Items: None
Party: Edgar, Sabin, Celes
Party's level: 17-22
=============================================================================

Now head towards the town of Kohlingen which is located northwest from Figaro 
castle and head towards the pub. You will see Setzer in his chair, talk to 
him as he will be surprised that you are alive. Celes wants Edgar to come 
with them but he doesn't have it anymore, its a world too chaotic for him and 
he has lost his wings. Celes then finally convinces Setzer to come along with 
them. Setzer wants to visit Daryl's tomb as he will get the party another 
one...airship that is! The game will automatically tell you where Daryl's 
tomb is, so head for that direction.

=============================================================================
ANOTHER AIRSHIP AWAITS AND A TRAGIC PAST
Items: Exp.Egg, Man Eater, Crystal Mail, Czarina Gown, Genji Helmet
Party: Edgar, Celes, Sabin
Party's level: 17-22
=============================================================================

Here inside Setzer opens up the door under Daryl's tomb, someone which Setzer 
knew in his past. Enter in the tomb and continue through to basement 2. Now 
head for the top right door and check the tombstone to reveal a door, and hit 
the switch to let loose the water. Then head towards the bottom left door and 
pick up the CRYSTAL MAIL, continue on and pick up the CZARINA GOWN. In the 
next room hit the switch and then head back towards basement 2. Then take the 
bottom right door and pick up a GENJI HELMET, and head back to basement 2 and 
take the middle room. In this room take the turtle through to the next room 
and then hit the switch, but don't take the turtle ride yet, go to the bottom 
room and in here there are four tombstones. They read:

                     UARE            ISSQ
                  
                     ORLD            THEW

Can you guess what it is trying to say? Yes that's right "THE WORLD IS
SQUARE" Pretty catchy and inventive huh? Now head back to basement 2 and take 
the top left door and carve something in the tombstone. Carve in 
"THEWORLDISSQUARE" and it will reveal the location of the EXP.EGG relic in 
Daryl's tomb. You do not need to go through the tomb finding and tomb writing 
to actually obtain the EXP.EGG relic, you can get it without doing the 
puzzles, but its just funner this way! Now head back to the middle door in 
basement 2 and continue on through to the next save point. Here don't pick up 
any treasure chests, but do save your game and heal your wounds if any. Check 
the treasure chest to the right inside is a Presenter.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
BOSS BATTLE: Presenter     HP: 9,845     ITEM: Dragon Claw
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
This boss is pretty hard, but he's like the first boss you faced at the
beginning of the game. Hit the aprt with the treasure chest and do not hit 
the shell otherwise recieve a nasty Magnitude8 quake attack. Keep your HP 
above 600, otherwise the GigaVolt will get you unless you have something that 
can obsorb lightning attacks. When he goes into his shell heal your party 
members and wait for him to pop out of his shell and then attack him. Keep 
this same pattern until he's gone.

Afterwards check the other treasure chest to the right and pick up a MAN
EATER dagger, then save your game and heal your wounds if neccessary. Now
make your way towards the next room  and check Daryl's tomb, but as the party 
does another boss attacks them.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
BOSS BATTLE: Dullahan     HP: 23,450
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
This boss will be tough. He will use Level? Pearl, if your levels are not 
divisible by 2 then you should be fine. He will use Ice 3 and Pearl in this 
battle, and there isn't really much that you can do about it except bring 
that character back to life and heal them. Don't use Ice magic in this battle 
because it will heal him, use Fire magic and keep pounding away with Sabin's 
Suplex or Pummel, Setzer's Slot attack, have Celes use Runic occasionally 
because this boss uses a lot of magic and have Edgar use his Chainsaw.

After the battle the door behind the tomb will open. Continue on through and 
inside the music changes as Setzer has a retrospect of old memories. A 
flashback occurs, and an expierimental airship might prove unstable, but 
Daryl decides to go anyways and tells Setzer that if anything should happen 
to her the Falcon is his. But Setzer thinks he will win it from her in a 
race, the scene then shifts towards the flashback of Setzer's view in his
flying airship as the two race head to head. Daryl wants to be the only woman 
who came closest to the stars as Setzer will wait for her on their hill 
before sunset. Daryl never showed up, a year later after the two's race the 
wreck of the Falcon was found. 

Setzer had found the airship and restored it and place it near Daryl's tomb, 
he couldn't bare to look at it because of what it did to Daryl, but it might 
be the thing that will save not only the party, but bring a new sense of hope 
to all living in the world(notice the music change, upbeat and its time to 
put a pounding on Kefka). The airship rises out of the waters and the party 
can attack Kefka from the air, but before they can do so they will need to 
find their friends. Then a bird comes by and Celes wants Setzer to follow it, 
she doesn't know why, so Setzer does and the party lands in the town of 
Maranda.

=============================================================================
THE TOWN OF MIRANDA AND THE MYSTERIOUS MAN
Items: None
Party: Celes, Setzer, Sabin, Edgar
Party's level: 19-22
=============================================================================

In here talk to the lady to the right of the armors shop and she will show 
you some rather useful information, something you can use! Although they are 
only views of each location, there is something that you can do once your 
done obtaining your next party member. Here in this town the people describe 
a strange man who kept calling people "thou" but can it be Cyan? Then talk to 
Lola in the house to the far right of town, inside she said someone sent her 
flowers all hand made of silk from Mobliz, including a letter, but wasn't 
Molbiz demolished by Kefka's beam of light?

Then read the letter and the handwriting looks a lot like Cyan's, but where
is it coming from. Lola will ask to attach the reply to a carrier pigeon, 
so will you? Of course! Take it to the bird just outside the house to the 
left and it will show you where it is going, follow that bird to the next
destination.

=============================================================================
RETURN TO ZOZO
Items: Rust-Rid(Key Item)
Party: Edgar, Sabin, Celes, Setzer
Party's level: 19-22
=============================================================================

Here when you enter Zozo talk to the carrier pigeon and it will fly off,
follow that bird to the top of this town. But first you can't get through
since the door at the top is locked, talk to the walking merchant in this
town and he will sell you the Rust-Rid for 1000 GP to open the door, do so 
and continue through to the top of the pub and onto Mt.Zozo.

=============================================================================
JOURNEY THROUGH MT.ZOZO
Items: Ice Shield, Gold Hairpin, ed Cap, Aegis Shield, Thunder Shield
Party: Celes, Sabin, Setzer, Edgar
Party's level: 19-22
=============================================================================

Here continue to the left and pick up the ICE SHLD and RED CAP and continue 
down. Also note that there will be this bear that you will encounter in 
random battles and will steal a CHUNK of your money, defeat it quickly and 
you will win back your money, if not he will escape and your hard earned 
money will be forever gone. Then pick up the THUNDER SHLD and equip it, then 
continue towards the top and pick up the AEGIS SHLD and equip it then head 
for the door to the left and outside is a GOLD HAIRPIN relic, then go back 
inside and take the right path. 

Outside make your way through pass the rope bridge and onto the next cave and 
to the left is a save point. Save your game and heal your wounds. NOTE: You 
can hit the switch at the top right to reveal a Storm Dragon if you want, but
I must warn you that its QUITE POWERFUL, so ignore that top switch for now 
and if you do want to fight it, check my strategies in the Side Areas down 
below. Now continue through down and make your way to the room with the silk 
flowers. Read the letter Cyan is about to send to Lola and you will discover 
that her boyfriend passed away sometime ago and he begs for her forgiveness 
as he wants her to make a new start with her life. 

Now make your way to the right and Cyan will send another letter to Lola. The
party then grett themselves to Cyan as they have not seen each other for so 
long and Cyan will automatically decide to go with the party, Cyan wonders 
how the party found him and he believes that the party has been reading his 
letters and quickly goes inside the cave and removes the flowers and letter 
and claims that all of this was just a diversion of his. But we all know that 
it was no diversion scheme, he had passed through Miranda and heard about 
Lola and felt sorry for her. 

She had sent letters everyday and recieved no reply, and Cyan being the noble 
hearted man that he is decides to pretend to be her boyfriend. He saw a 
similarity between her and him, they were both looking behind, but something 
then changed. He had also bumped into Gau in Maranda, and Gau wanted to 
become stronger if he was to face Kefka and most likely he had returned to 
the Veldt. Now head back to the right side of the mountain where Cyan was and 
pick up the key to Cyan's treasure chest. Inside the treasure chest is a rare 
item, a book about machinery and a "Book of Secrets." Now head out of Mt.Zozo 
and out of Zozo and back to your airship.

=============================================================================
TERRA COME BACK!
Items: Ether
Party: Whomever
Party's level: 20-23
=============================================================================

On your airship Cyan is in the engine room just dazzled over the machinery on 
the Falcon, talk to him if you want to change party members. Then when you 
are done head towards Mobliz and find Terra. In here Terra is not in her 
house, and it appears that Katarin ran off as Duane was a bit angry. Go to 
the house on the left side of Mobliz and watch the dog carefully. Follow that 
dog downstairs and you will see Terra, Katarin is about to have a baby and 
Duane comes in and apologizes. He hasn't been the best husband but he is 
learning and wants Katarin to come back with him. Then suddenly the whole 
place shakes as Phunbaba returns. Now you must right against Phunbaba again.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
BOSS BATTLE: Phunbaba      HP: 26,000
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
This battle is the same like last time, lose him a certain amount of HP and 
he will use his BabaBreath and blow two party members away.

After the battle Terra comes and decides to help out the party as she turns 
into her esper form.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
BOSS BATTLE: Phunbaba      HP: 26,000
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
This battle should be the same through and out. Have Terra use her magic and 
have the other party members attack regularly.

After the battle the kids see Terra and run back in fear, but the little girl 
notices that she is Terra. The children are not afraid of Terra anymore and 
she understands what she has been burying for so long..."love." She realizes 
that she must fight for the future of the children, she gives her goodbyes to 
Katarin and Duane and to the children, and Terra has discovered a new part of 
her she never understood until now and she will fight for the people who have 
not even been born yet. Now head back to your airship and rearrange your new 
party and head towards the Veldt which is north of Mobliz.

=============================================================================
GAU SMART, GAU COME BACK STRONG!
Items: None
Party: Whomever(must have three party members ONLY!)
Party's level: 20-23
=============================================================================

Here on the Veldt walk into a random encounter, also make sure that you only 
have three members in your party, if you have four then Gau won't come to 
you. When you go into a random encounter win the battle and Gau will come at 
the end and will travel with you now. After you are done head to the cave on 
the southwestern part of the Veldt.

=============================================================================
SHADOW, RELM, I DON'T KNOW!
Items: Striker, Rage-Ring
Party: Whomever
Party's level: 20-23
=============================================================================

In here when you enter Interceptor will see you and it appears that he wants 
you to follow him. So follow him and in this next room there are thieves near 
a fire, talk to them and they will tell you SPECIFICALLY how to acquire Gau 
if you had not done so yet, so if you can't interpret their words and still 
don't understand you are pretty slow! Continue through and pick up the 
treasure chest to the left and inside it contains a RAGE RING relic. There is 
also another treasure chest which contains TIGER FANGS for Sabin, but its 
guarded by an Allo Ver. 

After that make your way through to the bottom staircase. And continue to go 
through the stairs until you reach a door with a switch to the right of it. 
Hit the switch and pick up the STRIKER and then continue through to the right 
and you should eventually reach a save point, so save your game and heal your 
wounds. Then make your way to the next room you will see Shadow(or Relm if 
Shadow did not jump off with you on the Floating Continent). Then suddenly 
the party is attacked!
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
BOSS BATTLE: SirBehemoth(2)      HP: 19,000    
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
This battle will be difficult, cause you will have to face off against the 
two of them. Have Terra and Celes use Fire magic on the first SirBehemoth and 
have Cyan use his SwdTech, Sabin his Blitz(pummel or Suplex), Gau anyone of 
his rage attacks, Setzer his regular attacks or Slots, and have Edgar use his 
Drill in this battle. Keep doing this until the first one dies and then 
another one will attack from behind. This time continue the same pattern but 
have Celes and Terra use Ice magic against the 2nd SirBehemoth. After 
defeating the two you will recieve a BEHEMOTHSUIT and CRUSTAL SHLD.

After the battle the party takes Shadow(or Relm) to Thamasa where he can heal 
his wounds. Then a flashback occurs to Shadow's past where he left out of 
town and Interceptor follows. 

NOTE: If you saved Relm a different scenario will take place obviously.
      Now leave towards Jidoor which is south of Zozo on the western part of
      the world map.

=============================================================================
OWZER
Items: Moogle Suit, Relic Ring, 2000GP, Potion, Ether, Remedy
Party: Whomever
Party's level: 21-24
=============================================================================

Here head straight for the mansion up top to Owzer's house. Inside here head 
straight up and turn on the lights. Then head to the left and you will notice 
that the paintings are different from last time. Now check the bottom left 
portrait of the lady and two Dahlings will attack you, defeat them and a door 
will replace their portrait. Enter through to the next room and head 
downstairs, here in this room a portrait will attack you and you will have to 
fight off against a SoulDancr and four Wild Cat(s). 

After defeating them head to the left door up top to pick up a MOOGLE SUIT
