and then head for the right door. Here head straight up and go behind the
three doors to pick up a RELIC RING. Here the three doors will open and close 
and only one of them will open at a time. Ignore the two doors on the right 
and head for the left door and continue on through to the room with the 
floating treasure chests. Try to reach for them and a battle will ensue. 

The treasure chest include 2000 GP which is guarded by a Soul Dancr and four 
Wild Cats, a POTION which is also guarded by a Soul Dancr and four Wild Cats, 
an ETHER which is also guarded again by a Soul Dancr and four Wild Cats, and 
finally a REMEDY which is once again gaurded by a Soul Dancr and four Wild 
Cats. After picking those treasure chests up check the middle painting a a 
fight against a StillLife will ensue, defeat it and a door will replace the 
portrait, and enter through to the next room.

In this next room there are two doors and a save point, save your game and
heal your wounds. Now enter the door on the right and talk to Owzer, he tells 
you that there is a monster inside the painting and that the party cannot 
attack the painting because it means too much to Owzer, then Relm is startled 
by the presence of Chadarnook who came out of the painting.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
BOSS BATTLE: Chadarnook     HP: 30,000(each)
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
This boss is extremely tough. He will use Phantasm on the party which is 
sorta like a poison attack that constantly drains your HP. Lose him a few HP 
and he will change form and this form will use Bolt 2 and Bolt 3. So if you 
have a THUNDER SHLD or AEGIS SHLD equipped that shouldn't be much of a 
problem. Have Cyan use his SwdTech, have Sabin use his Suplex or Pummel, have 
Edgar use his Drill, have Setzer use his Slot attack, have Gau use anyone of 
his Rage attacks, and have Terra and Celes use magic or attack as normal.

After the battle Relm tells the party to relax and Owzer thanks the party for 
saving the painting in which he thinks is more precious than his own life. 
The monster was in the portrait because Owzer had bought a stone from the 
auction house and he suddenly felt like painting a picture of a Starlet, but 
he could never paint it since it was out of his league, but then he found 
Relm, whose artistic abilities surpassed those of anybody Owzer has ever seen 
in his life. 

He then tells you that the stone is over by the bookshelf, so check the 
bookshelf and you will recieve the Magicite Starlet in which Owzer is more 
than happy to get rid of. Relm then decides to leave and she tells Owzer that 
she will be back to finish the painting. Now head back to your airship and 
head towards the giant star shaped mountain in the middle of the world map, 
a top the southern continent.

=============================================================================
THE CAVE TO THE LOST TREASURE
Items: Wing Edge, Ribbon, Draon Horn, Warp Stone
Party: Whomever
Party's level: 22-25
=============================================================================

You should see a small spot in which you can land your airship, when you land 
or at least try to, Setzer will tell you that you will need to split up into 
two groups. So do so, and afterwards you will land atop the Pheonix Cave, you 
can switch between the two groups using the Square button or the "Y" button 
if you are playing the SNES version.

NOTE: This place is very complicated and I will try to be as detailed as
      possible, but most likely you will be better off doing this yourself
      instead of following this guide. But for those who are really stuck
      read along as I will tell you EVERYTHING that is in this cave.

Now enter inside and have the first group step on the switch and switch to
group 2 to have them go through the door on the left. After group 2 has gone 
through have them step on the switch that is above the switch group 1 is on. 
Switch to group 1 and have them take the right path and hit the switch above 
to remove the spikes. Now switch to group 2 and move through the path that 
has been removed of spikes(don't take the treasure chest to the left yet 
otherwise you will fall to the bottom spikes below) and walk to the right and 
down the stairs to the switch, step on the switch and the spikes on the floor 
will be removed, now switch to group 1. 

Now walk through and to the next room, the treasure chest to the right 
doesn't contain anything. Now walk up top and the treasure chest contains 
nothing so don't bother with it and hit the switch which will reveal three 
stepping stones over the magma. Now switch to group 2, and take the top left 
staircase. Here in the Magma room go down and take the staircase up to the 
next room and hit the switch that will create a bridge leading to the WING 
EDGE, the bridge is here so that you do not fall to the spikes below. Then go
back to the next room and take the stepping stone path, don't get the
treasure chest just yet and hit the switch that you see. 

Now switch to group 1 and have them take the path that was opened and go to 
the switch that you saw above the rock and step on the switch and the rock 
will move out of the way for group 2. Now switch to group 2 and head towards 
the next room. In this room there is a save point to the left, so save your 
game and heal your wounds. Now step on the switch above and switch to group 
1. Now walk around the path and onto the next room. Here you will have to use 
the stepping stones to make your way across around to the next room, and yes
there are still no treasures in the treasure chests. 

Here in this room hit the switch and the water will drop below and cool off 
the magma, now switch back to group 2, now have this group hit the switch to 
the left which will clear the rocks for group 1, now switch to group 1. Now 
continue down and you will see a dragon wandering around, ignore it and pick 
up the DRAGON HORN relic and its optional if you want to fight the dragon. 
But if you do refer to my Side Areas section on how to beat him. Whether you
choose to or not, do up the stairs and stand on the switch that reveals two 
rocks. Now switch back to group 2 and have them walk to the left side and to 
the magma room that had been cooled off. 

In this room you can pick up your first treasure chest which is a RIBBON and 
then continue onto the top left room and walk across the two rocks and now 
you should be with the other group. Hit either switch at the bottom and 
switch to group 1 and have them hit the other switch. Now continue through to 
the bottom and in the next room the party will meet up with Locke. Locke has 
discovered a legendary relic that can restore life, it has been weakened over 
time due to the large cracks in the stone. 

Locke feels that his life has no purpose ever since that incident with 
Rachel, but he wants to right the wrong that he had made. Locke decides to go 
with the party, but only as far as Kohlingen, he then sets the stone near 
Rachel, but nothing happens. But after a rather unuseful remark by the 
Patriarch and stone begins to glow and Rachel awakens as she has been 
dreaming of Locke as she wanted to hear Locke's voice. However the Pheonix 
has only given Rachel very little time and she must leave soon, but she wants 
to tell Locke something. 

The times she spent with Locke she was happy and at the moment the incident
occured she only thought of Locke and will never forget Locke and the joy 
that he has brought her. As Rachel is about to leave she tells Locke that he 
must forget about the past and stay true to himself as Rachel gives the power 
of the Pheonix to Locke. She then leaves Locke and the power of the Pheonix 
now inscribes along Locke. When locke leaves to the room above Celes is with 
him, but Locke has a new sense of hope and now its time to stop Kefka once 
and for all. 

As Locke and Celes leaves, Locke remembers something. He hands over the the 
treasures that he had found in the Pheonix Cave(that explains why all those 
treasure chests were empty), X-POTION, FENIXDOWN, X-ETHER, ELIXIR, FLAME 
SHLD, and a VALIANTKNIFE. The party has an appointment with Kefka, but don't 
head to the tower yet. Head towards Thamasa where you had left Shadow, its on 
a small island at the bottom right corner of the world map.

=============================================================================
WHERE'S SHADOW?
Items: None
Party: Whomever
Party's level: 24-28
=============================================================================

In Thamasa Shadow is gone(or Relm) and people in town say he is headed for 
the Colleseum, or has already done so. So head to the Colleseum.

NOTE: If you did not save Shadow head towards Jidoor, use the Owzer
      walkthrough to get you to Relm.

=============================================================================
SHADOW WAIT UP!
Items: None
Party: Whomever
Party's level: 24-28
=============================================================================

The Colleseum is in the northwest part of the world map at the very tip. It 
looks a bit like the Opera house on the outside so don't be fooled by it. 
Inside you will see a familiar face, wait a minute...is that Ultros? Ha! 
Let's take this minute to laugh at him! You also learn here that you can bet 
items for prizes, in fact there are a lot of different combinations here, and 
I do mean A LOT! But for now head towards the Colleseum's battle arena and 
bet the STRIKER daggar(hopefully you did not sell it!) and a battle against 
Shadow will start. This battle should be pretty easy since Shadow has no 
armor or weapons to defeat you with. After the battle Shadow tells the party 
that the only thing he knew how to do was fight. He then decides to go with 
the party, so now head back to your airship and head for the magic tower.

=============================================================================
STRAGO WAKE UP YOU BONEHEAD!
Items: None(yet)
Party: Relm and whomever
Party's level: 24-28
=============================================================================

The Magic Tower is on the same island as Mobliz is, its west of Mobliz and 
its comepltely surrounded by high terrain and mountains and the only way 
through is buy airship. Land your airship near it and make sure you have Relm 
in your group. Inside Relm will immediately yell at Strago and then he 
awakens from his brainwash and is surprised to see alive. Of course Relm is 
alive "you idiot!" Did you think she would check out before the old man? 
Afterwards Strago makes himself at home on the airship, so now that everybody 
is back its time to lay the "SmackDown" on Kefka. Don't bother with this 
place yet, its VERY tough to get through even the first few floors at your 
state now, but for now head towards Kefka's tower via the airship.

=============================================================================
THE FINAL BATTLE AWAITS
Items: Rainbow Brush, Megalixir, Minerva, Tack Star, Force Armor, Ribbon,
       Fixed Dice, Red Cap, Nutkin Suit, Guantlet, Hero Ring, Aegis Shield,
Party: Whomever(split into three groups)
Party's level: 26-30
=============================================================================

NOTE: Before you head inside here I suggest you check out my Side Areas 
      section first. The side areas will significantly boost your levels and
      gain you some incredible weapons and armors and magicite. However, it
      is still very possible to beat the game without all the extras.

The battles that you are about to fight will drain you of your HP and MP 
rather quickly and you will need to stock up on materials like TENTs, 
POTIONs, and stuff like that before you go. Kefka's Tower is on the southern 
continent north of the town of Albrook. You can't enter it from the bottom, 
you must move in through with the airship. Land your airship on top of 
Kefka's tower, but Celes doesn't feel right about something. If they destroy 
the statues the very power that gives the espers life will kill the espers, 
and what will happen to Terra? 

You will now have to break your entire party into three groups. Split your 
party into any three groups that you want. Here you will start off with group 
1, you will need to switch between groups, but don't worry, you don't need to 
do it as intensively as the Pheonix Cave. From here go around and pick up the 
CORONET and then enter the next area. In here take the escalator down to the 
next area. In here pick up the FIXED DICE at the top and onto the next area 
outside and then continue onto the next area. 

In this room you will have to wait here. Go to your second party now. From 
here go around and down and over at the top left of this room pick up the 
MINERVA and go down to the bottom right and take the top room and inside pick 
up the TACK STAR and then continue on outside. Here in this room there is a 
monster to the far left, approach it and a fight will enuse.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
BOSS BATTLE: Atma    HP: 55,000
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
This boss is one tough customer. Watch for his Southern Cross attack, his 
Fire 3 attack, Bolt 3 attack, and his Clean Sweep attack. His physical  
attacks deal a good amount of damage at your point in levels right now but if 
you set up Golem you won't be harmed by his physical attacks. Have everybody 
use there best attacks or best magics like Ultima(if you have it) or Flare or 
Pearl or Ice 3 and so on. Keep your HP above 1300 if possible to survive his 
Meteor attack. NOTE: Mog can learn a new dance in this battle.

After the battle there will be a save point that will open up, so save your
game and heal your wounds. Then continue onto the next area make your way
around to the left and enter the next room. Here there are two pipes, ignore
the right pipe and enter the left pipe. Outside here make sure you pick up
the FORCE SHLD and then go down and enter the door on the left. Inside here
there is a RIBBON and you will also see group 1, step on the switch and the 
floor will make passage for group 1. Now go back and through the door to the 
right and keep going and you will see a dragon on top of the red platform, 
you can fight it if you want if you feel strong enough, but you can ignore 
him for now.

Then continue onto the room to the left and make your way to the next switch. 
You can step on it if you want, but for now switch to your third group. Now 
in group 3 keep going down and along the way pick up the RED CAP and enter 
the top room. In here keep going up and continue along the way and pick up a 
NUTKIN SUIT and a GUANTLET. Now go back outside and take the bottom room. 
Keep going and pick up a HERO RING relic along the way and move towards the 
top moving rail and in here there is a save point at the top left. So save 
your game and heal your wounds and continue on to the left. Before you can go 
anywhere a monster attacks you.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
BOSS BATTLE: Inferno & Striker & Rough     HP: 30,800(I) 8,000(R) 11,000(S)
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
This battle will be tough. It will most likely start the battle with the
Atomic Ray attack, which causes at max 1100 HP of damage to every character.
Keep your HP up and take out the Striker and Rough(its arms) first so that 
you don't have to deal with its Bolt attacks. Use all of your best attacks 
and keep pounding on him while keeping your HP up. Watch for his GigaVolt 
attack which can inflict over 2000 HP of damage.

After the battle continue on outside and out here pick up the MEGALIXIR and 
to the left pick up the RAINBOW BRSH and also hit the shining treasure chest 
to clear up the path to the left of you and then continue on. You will then 
see another dragon, fight it if you wish and if you do and need help refer to 
my guide below with the 8 Dragons. Whether you do or not continue onto the 
next area and step on the switch and the door will open up. Now switch back 
to your first group. Now in here continue onto the next area and make sure 
you pick up another TACK STAR along the way and then you will see your other 
two party members. 

Go up and step on the switch and go to either side, when you do the path will 
be blocked, but for now go to either side and drop the weight on the switch, 
but your party members must move out of the way first. After doing that 
switch to your other party and go up the now accessible stairs and do the 
same thing your first group did and drop the weight on the switch. Now switch 
to your other group and have them reach up the middle switch and stay there. 
Now have your other two party members hit the other switches, then when all
three groups are standing on the switches the door will open up. Now have 
your middle group go down and hit the switch again. This will open up the 
doors on the other two sides. Now continue up and go on to the middle room 
and a Guardian will be in your path.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
BOSS BATTLE: Guardian     HP: 60,000
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
At first when you encountered this guy you could not damage him and he would 
always beat you, but now you can damage him. You can damage him now but this 
guy is TOUGH. Heck he's the toughest boss in the game as of now. Use all of 
your most powerful attacks and magics and keep your HP up at max if possible 
and keep pouding away. Watch for its Entwine attack, it will cause slow, so 
use either Dispel or Fast to cure it.

After the battle a save point will open up, so save your game and heal your 
wounds and continue on. Keep going and then you will have to fight against 
another boss.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
BOSS BATTLE: Poltrgeist     HP: 58,000     ITEM: Aura Lance
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
This battle will be tough. Watch for it to use Meteo which will cause over 
2000 HP of damage to every character. Its Fire 3 attack and Southern Cross 
attack can be absorbed by a FLAME SHLD. USe your best magic and keep your HP 
up at max if possible and attack attack attack!

After the battle the continue on and in here is another save point. So save 
your game and continue on and in here step on the switch and switch to your 
other group. Here just continue on until you reach the next statue.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
BOSS BATTLE: Doom          HP: 63,000     ITEM: SKY RENDER
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
This battle will be very tough. Watch for its N.Cross attack, it will freeze 
your party members, but not all. Use low level fire magic attacks against 
your party members to defrost them. Watch for its Ice 3 attack as well, so if 
you have an ICE SHLD equipped you can absorb the attack or nullify it with 
your FLAME SHLD. Watch for it when it targets a party member, its preparing 
to use its Demon Rage attack, it will do at max 7500 HP of damage. However 
this can be nullified to just 1500 HP of damage if a party member is in the 
back row and having the Safe casted as well as wearing Force armor equipment 
with the Paladin Shld. 

After the battle a save point will appear, so save your game and heal your
wounds and continue onto the next room and step on the switch. Now switch to 
your next group.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
BOSS BATTLE: Goddess       HP: 44,000     ITEM: Excalibur
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
This battle will not be easy, even though you get the Pincer attack off in 
this battle. Watch for its Southern Cross, it will do a good deal of damage 
to your party members, so keep your HP up and above 700 just to be safe. Use 
your best magics and attack constantly while keeping a close eye on your HP 
and the battle should be won.

After the battle a save point will open up, so save your game and heal your 
wounds and continue onto the next room and step on the switch and you will be 
transported over to Kefka's domain at the top of this tower. Here when you 
enter Kefka has been expecting you, he appears in a magical triangle and uses 
his power and toys around with the party. But Terra tells him that people 
will keep rebuilding the things he takes from them, but Kefka doesn't care, 
he will destroy everything people build, he doesn't understand why people 
cling onto their lives when they know they won't live forever, but Terra 
tells him that its the day-to-day concerns, personal victories, the 
celebration of life and love. 

Kefka however doesn't like what he is hearing and asks if Terra has found her 
joy, and she has, she knows what love is. Locke has learned a great deal 
about life as well, Edgar's dream is to build a kingdom of freedom and 
dignity, Sabin has come and expierienced the caring that his brother has 
brought for him throughout his childhood, Celes has met someone who can 
accept her for who she is, Strago has a special little granddaughter, Relm 
has a brave grandpa that will stand with her at all times, Setzer's airship 
and Daryl's love, Mog has friends here as well(that what he would say if you 
have him in your party), Gau has friends that are by him right now. Kefka 
doesn't like what the party is telling him, it sickens him as they "sound 
like chapters from a self-help booklet!" 

Then Kefka uses his power and sends the beam of light towards the the world, 
he wants to destroy everything and create a monument of non-existence(does 
this sound a bit Exdeath-ish?), but Terra tells him that life will go on and 
that people will always have dreams. But Kefka will hunt them down, Locke 
will not allow him to harm another living thing, then Kefka sends another 
beam of light towards the world. 

Now you will have to set up an order in which the party members will fight in 
1-12, but if you have been following the walkthrough then there are only 11 
members in your party. You will face off in four battles each are very tough, 
if one of your characters die during battle, the next character up will 
replace that character until all of your party members lose or if you win all 
four battles. After you're done a battle will ensue:
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
FINAL BATTLE 1: (Kefka Demon) & (Demon's hands)   HP: 30,000(KD) 60,000(BH)
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
Here in this battle have Cyan use his SwdTech, have Sabin use his Pummel, 
have Terra use her regular attacks or magic and the same goes for Celes, have 
Gau use any one of his rage attacks, have Setzer use his Slot attack (its 
better if you use the Coin Toss relic and use GP Rain instead), have Edgar 
use his CrossBow, have Locke attack as normal, have Strago use his AquaRake 
attack or attack with magic, and have Relm attack as normal and use magic. 
Once you knock out the hands have Edgar use his Drill against the Kefka 
demon. He will use R.Polarity at the beginning of the match and that will 
draw you closer to him and make his physical attacks cause more damage, there 
is nothing that you can do about this besides casting Safe on the party or 
hope that he will miss with its attacks because they are VERY powerful.

After this battle another tough battle will ensue.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
FINAL BATTLE 2: (Outergate Demon)     HP: 112,000(combined)
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
In this next battle its the same as the last one, this time you will have to 
deal with four targets instead of three and you will be back in your previous 
positions as the R.Polarity effect has worn off from your last battle. Keep 
your HP at max if possible and you might want to use Haste to quicken your 
party and make quick decisions otherwise you can find yourself having an 
early deathwish. If you knock out one of the targets it will use the last 
attack 10 Hits, the attacks are pretty powerful considering at what levels 
you are at right now, so you may want to switch your party members to the 
back ranks prior to destroying any one of the targets.

After this battle the next battle will ensue.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
FINAL BATTLE 3: (Unearthly Standstill)     HP: 9,999(Girl) 40,000(sleep)
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
This battle is the EASIEST of the three battles so far. However you must heal 
immediately after it uses the White Wind attack at the beginning of the 
battle because as you can expect it will put your HP at near fatal condition. 
Attack normally like the battles above and keep your HP up above 1000, or to 
its max because the Meteo attack(yes that's right, not Meteor) will cause a 
great deal of damage against the party. Make your decisions quick and keep 
your rythmn going and you should win this battle. Also note that there are 
only two targets, one of the targets(I forgot which one specifically) is 
easily taken out with a few hits. Also even though you destroy this boss, it 
will use Calmness as its final attack and take out one party member.

After the battle the music from the beginning of the game(you know before you 
even begin playing the part with Vicks and Wedge) and this is your last 
battle.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
FINAL CONFRONTATION: Kefka       HP: 62,000
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
Kefka doesn't even know where hope and dreams come from, these things he
believes that he is going to destroy and then gives his menacing laugh. This 
battle will be tough. The methods for beating him are the same as like the 
previous battles, but keeping your HP up to the max is a definite must. (the 
music in here starts to get I don't know a bit Lavos-ish wouldn't you 
agree?)He will use the Fallen One attack that reduces your entire party's HP 
to 1, so immediately heal. I would also like to note that his Goner attack 
does massive damage, but that's not the impressive thing about it, I'm 
talking about the special effects!

=============================================================================

                                   ------
                                   Ending
                                   ------

  NOTE: This is a spoiler, and as you can tell from my FF7 FAQ and FF2 FAQ
        I do this all the time. So if you do not want to know the ending of
        the game then turn away now!...What did I just tell you? Go... Your
        still reading this huh?...Whoever is reading this is a bamma...heh,
        I guess that means you!

After the battle with Kefka the whole place is about to collapse. Then (put 
party member who was on airship) comes in and tells the party that the 
airship is just ahead(note that since you only have 11 party members you will 
just escape without anyone coming in, but if you came here with 10 party 
members then that party meber will alert you to escape, same thing if you 
have 14 party members). Terra then transforms into her esper state and 
collapses, then the magicite the party was carrying diperses off into the 
air. Magic is starting to die from the world and the magicites can't even 
exist, but does this mean that Terra will die out to? 

I mean she is half human. Terra then gets up and will lead the party out with 
her last ounce of strength. A picture of a book is shown in superior 
graphical quality that looks almost lifelike and Cyan is seen escaping while 
pushing out the mechanical legions that block the way for Edgar. Then Setzer
bumps into a wall that opens up the paths on both sides, then the door on the 
left explodes and they party goes the other way, sometimes you just have to 
feel your way through each situation. Sabin holds up a giant piece of metal 
that nearly kills his brother, but he knew that Edgar be the better king and 
he didn't even know why he had the stupid muscles.

Mog then suddenly almost falls hanging on to dear life as the floor collapse 
as Edgar pick up Mog by the hair, in which Mog hates. Umaro then busts a way 
open for Setzer and Celes as the door in front of them is blocked and cheers 
afterwards. Gogo however has to mimic Celes as Setzer and Edgar are blocked 
off, he does the exact same thing Celes does as they move on. Gau on the 
other hand shows Edgar and Celes a shortcut to the bottom path below as he 
tosses them down, pretty funny if you ask me! Locke, Celes, Terra, and Setzer 
and Edgar escaped but Celes nearly falls on her way, but Locke saves her and 
promises that he will not let go. 

Terra on her way out has the last piece of magicite disappear as her father 
Maduin tells her that if her human side is strong enough she will be able to 
live on as a human being on the world. Relm saves Strago as he is too old to 
catch up, but luckily Relm is strong enough to carry him! Shadow then tells 
Interceptor to go as he runs off and decides that he will start over again. 
Strago however tries to reach for the pulley, but after a couple of tries Old 
Man can jump! Then the game thanks you, and so do I for respecting this FAQ 
hopefully.

The party must hurry out, as Terra shows them the way as the last piece of
magicite turns to dust and Terra's power is fading. The scene shifts towards 
the kids from Mobliz and Katarin can be seen having a baby. The party on the 
other hand is knocked out but slowly get up, and Terra has fallen aboard 
thanks to Setzer. Now the credits roll up as the airship strolls through 
beautiful environments showing off the graphical Mode 7 power of the SNES(in 
my opinion they beat anything to date!). The crystal theme from FFIV comes up 
and Katarin's baby has just arrived in a new world of dreams and hope. 

The kids in Mobliz walk out and greet Terra, the scene shifts towards Thamasa 
as the burned house is being rebuilt. In another town a plant is growing and 
in Figaro Castle the pople are moving around in activity, Terra then stands 
at port bow and lets her air fly through the wind as the doves that fly by 
move towards the land as new life is being brought upon the land and a quick 
shot and almost life-like shot of the Falcon is seen flying off.

Afterwards the FMV ending plays. You will also be asked if you want to create 
a system file prior to the FMV ending, doing so means all of the Bonus 
sections you have unlocked will be saved to a memory card.

                                 ----------
                                 Side Areas
                                 ----------

  Well as you can expect since FF5 had so MANY side areas FF6 would have a
  great deal right? Yes! There are plenty of things to do after you have
  beaten the game, and I'm here to help you complete all of them!

=============================================================================
THE 8 DRAGONS AND CRUSADER
Items: None
Party: Whomever
Recommended level: 32
=============================================================================

Remember when you were in Mt.Zozo and I told you not to fight that Wind 
Dragon? Well if you listened and haven't done so head back to the place and
hit the switch to reveal the Wind Dragon and make sure you have some strong
magic and also that you have a THUNDER SHLD equipped. Then go near the Dragon 
and a fight will ensue.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
DRAGON BATTLE: Storm Dragon     HP: 42,000     ITEM: Force Armor
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
This battle here will be very tough, but if you can defeat the MagiMaster you 
can win this battle as well. Keep your HP above 800 and pound it with your 
regular attacks. Use Ultima if you have it or Meteor, Flare, or Pearl. Have 
Sabin use his Bum Rush(or any other of his Blitz attacks) and have Cyan use 
his level 7 SwdTech to deal monster damage, have Edgar use his Drill(if you 
are at level 80 this can deal over 8000 HP of damage with every hit!) and 
have Gau use one of his rages. Have Gogo mimic a strong attack(E.G. Ultima, 
Drill, etc.), have Mog use his best Dance, have Strago use his GrandTrain 
Lore attack, and have Relm attack with magic. Anybody equipped with the 
THUNDER SHLD will take no damage from his Wind Slash attack and you will 
absorb any of his lightning attacks.

After the battle there are now 7 dragons left. Did you remember when you were 
in the Pheonix Cave there was a dragon walking around? In case you did not 
choose to fight it, head back once you are strong enough and go near it and a 
fight will ensue.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
DRAGON BATTLE: Red Dragon      HP: 30,000     ITEM: Strato
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
This battle here will be very tough just like the first battle. He will use a 
lot of Fire magic as you can expect and also as you can expect hit him with 
Ice magic to deal heavy damage. If you are wearing an armor that protects 
against Fire or absorbs fire that should do you well. He will use Fire 2 and 
Fire 3 at times and his regular attacks will do mild damage, not much that 
will get you concerned over anything. Use Ultima, Meteo, Flare, Pearl, or Ice 
3 to damage him. Contiue this pattern and keep your HP above 1000, so that 
his Fire 3 attack won't get you.

After the battle there are now 6 dragons left. Head towards Narche and along 
the northern mines there is a dragon wandering around, just walk near it and 
a fight will ensue.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
DRAGON BATTLE: Ice Dragon      HP: 24,400     ITEM: Force Shield
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
Here in this battle hit it with everything you've got. Fire magic works real 
well in this battle as you can expect and use Ultima, Meteo, Flare, or Pearl 
to damage it if you don't have a Fire 3 magic. He will use his Absolute 0 
attack, so watch for it and keep your HP above 500. Also when your party 
members are frozen use fire magic on them to free them, if he gets your 
entire party with it, there is literally nothing you can do about it. Keep 
hacking away and he should be gone.

After the battle there are now 5 dragons left. Now head for the Magic Tower 
in which you acquired Strago in and at the third part of the tower there is a 
room in which you got the STUNNER in, a dragon is in that room go to it and a 
fight will ensue.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
DRAGON BATTLE: White Dragon      HP: 18,500      ITEM: Pearl Lance
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
This battle will be pretty tough. Don't use Pearl in this battle because it 
will absorb it, so use Ultima, Meteo, or Flare. Keep your HP above 1200 and 
keep pounding him with your magic attacks like Fire 3 or Ice 3. He will start 
the battle off with two consecutive Pearl attacks and they will do about 1100 
HP of damage. Keep using Ultima in this battle and he will counter with 
Dispel, if you cna keep a constant chain of Ultima spells he will seldom pull 
off his Pearl attack! 

After the battle you will recieve the PEARL LANCE. Now there are just four 
dragons left. Now go to Figaro Castle and ask the driver to go to Figaro and 
he will say that something is odd about the stratum. Refer to the Odin's 
reign section of the Side Area to tell you exactly where the next dragon is.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
DRAGON BATTLE: Water Dragon      HP: 26,900
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
Here in this battle your lighting attacks will do well against him. Have
Sabin use his Aurabolt, and have any other of the characters use lightning
based attacks or their best and most damaging attacks. Keep your HP above
500 otherwise its Clean Sweep attack will get you. Keep this process up until 
you've won. NOTE: If Clean Sweep is used on Strago here in this battle he 
will learn it. Its a more powerful version of AquaRake.

Now there are 3 dragons left. Head for the Opera House on the southwestern
part of the world map to face off against your next dragon. In here talk to 
the Impressario and he will tell you that a dragon is sitting smack in the 
middle of the stage. Head for the switch room at the top right and hit the 
second switch from the right and you will fall to the floor below and a fight 
will ensue.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
DRAGON BATTLE: Dirt Dragon      HP: 28,500     ITEM: Magus Rod
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
This battle will be tough. Cast Float(you should do this before battle) to 
every party member in here so you can avoid his Quake and Magnitude8 attack. 
If you don't you will suffer at least 1800 HP of damage from his Quake attack 
and about 1100 from his Magnitude8 attack. After you are on Float status all 
you have to worry about are his physical attacks which do only about 400 HP 
of damage, and his Slide attack which does about 700 HP of damage to every 
party member. So keep your HP up and keep attacking him with your strongest 
attacks like Ultima, Flare, Pearl you know the real deal. Keep this up and 
you should win the battle.

After the battle it looks like the Impressario will have to save the world
again. There are now only two dragons left. So where are they? The two last
dragons are on Kefka's Tower silly! The second group in Kefka's Tower will
fight the Gold Dragon.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
DRAGON BATTLE: Gold Dragon      HP: 32,400      ITEM: Crystal Orb
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
Yes I know, it doesn't look like a dragon to me. It looks more like a 
dinosaur, but who cares. This battle will be tough, it uses only lightning 
attacks like GigaVolt, Bolt 3, Bolt 2, and Bolt. Its Bolt attacks do a lot
of damage, but having the Thunder Shld equipped in this battle will make the 
battle go by like a breeze. Hit him with your most powerful magics and keep 
your HP up at all times and hopefully he will be gone.

After the battle there is only 1 dragon left. The third group will face off 
against the last dragon.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
DRAGON BATTLE: SKULL DRAGON     HP: 32,800     ITEM: Muscle Belt
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
This battle will be pretty tough. Since this dragon is undead it has a 
weakness against fire. Use your most powerful fire spells and other magic 
spells. Watch for its Disaster attack, it will make a party member be 
infected with every negative status effect in the book, but having either the 
RIBBON or PALADIN SHLD equipped will counteract those effects. Keep your HP 
and attack fast otherwise you will be knocked out with its Condemned attack.

That's it! You now have Crusader, a very power Esper and you can learn
Merton, a really powerful spell that's on par with Ultima! Congratulations!

=============================================================================
ACQUIRING GOGO
Items: Hero Ring, Thunder Shield, Zyphyr Cape, Tack Star, Ether, Magical
       Brush, Red Jacket, Genji Armor, Fake Mustache
Party: Whomever
Recommended level: 30
=============================================================================

Take your airship to the small island on the top right corner of the world
and walk into a random encounter and you should meet up with a ZoneEater and 
let it Engulf the entire party. After it Engulfs the entire party you will be 
under the island. In here don't go up, its the exit out of here and since you 
didn't do anything here then why would you want to leave? Take the stairs 
down and in this area walk towards the left and jump your way across. Watch 
for the walking green men though, don't try to talk to them because all they 
will do is push you to the floor below and you will have to make your way 
back up. 

Along the way pick up the GENJI ARMOR, MAGICAL BRUSH, and a FAKEMUSTACHE. But 
if you do get bumped off make sure you pick up the RED JACKET and an ETHER. 
Then continue onto the next room which contains a save point, save your game 
and heal your wounds if any. Then make your way to the next room, in this 
room its a bit tricky. The ceiling will constantly drop and move up, avoid 
getting crushed and move to each treasure chest and STAY IN FRONT OF THE 
TREASURE CHEST! That is primarily the safest position in the room, pick up 
the ZEPHYR CAPE and HERO RING(NOTE: Having the Sprint Shoes really helps in 
here). 

NOTE: The third treasure chest in the room which is on the far left of the 
      room IS NOT SAFE! Do not stay in front of it otherwise you will get 
      crushed. What I do is after the second treasure chest I make my way 
      down to the bottom left of the room and wait for the ceiling to lift 
      up(with the help of the Sprint Shoes of course) and then pick up the 
      TACK STAR. 

Then continue onto the next room and in here you will have to hop across 
treasure chests, as you do make sure you hit the switch near the entrance of 
the room as well. In this room there is a THUNDER SHLD as well, then continue 
onto the next room and in here talk to the figure in the middle of the room:

  "Shrouded in odd clothing, ...is this a man...? ...a woman...? ...or should
   we ask...?

Here you will be given the chance to name this man or woman, just name him
Gogo and be on with it. Here he will mimic your actions in battle only if he 
deems you worthy, quite modest if you ask me. The party tells Gogo what they 
are doing here and he is a bit astonished by their tale and decides to help 
them out because they want to right the wrongs. Now that he is with you, you 
can have him in your party at any time by rearranging your party members on 
yur airship.

=============================================================================
DESPERATION ATTACKS
Items: NA
Party: NA
Recommended level: NA
=============================================================================

Okay I'm too lazy to list out all the attacks(actually there are only 12 in 
the game. Umaro, Gau, and Gogo do not have desperation attacks because they 
have no FIGHT commands. Basically when your HP is down and your character 
starts to show signs of fatigue, there is a 1/20 chance that the attack will 
come out. These desperation attacks are vastly powerful and often very worthy 
of eye candy. Enjoy!

=============================================================================
NARCHE, MOG, UMARO
Items: Rune Edge, Moogle Charm, Elixir, Cursed Shield, Ragnarok, 5000GP,
       Wall Ring, Hyper Wrist, Theif Knife, Sneak Ring
Party: Locke and whomever
Recommended level: 29
=============================================================================

Head to Narche and inside there is a wolf that will tell you that there is
basically nothing left to do here and only a treasure hunter can pick those
locks. Wait a minute, you do have Locke right? Good then have him in your
party. Now head to the weapons shop and go downstairs and talk to the old
man, he will give you a magicite, you can except it as the magicite Ragnarok
or have the sword Ragnarok, it doesn't matter. But I would take the sword
because if you have the Paladin Shield that means you can learn Ultima,
but the Ragnarok Esper can morph opponents into items. 

You decide, then head for the house above the relics shop and speak with the 
sick man downstairs and he will give you the CURSED SHIELD, he mentions if 
you can break its curse imagine its defense power! You can break the curse by
equipping the shield and winning 255 battles with it and it will turn into 
the PALADIN SHIELD. But with the load times of the PSX, good luck! Ha! If you 
do equip the CURSED SHIELD make sure you have the RIBBON relic on as well, 
you can stop everything except for the Condemned status, and you must wear it 
and win battles as well. 

Now head to the west side of town to the mines through the old man's house 
from earlier in the game and find that moogle cave you found earlier in the 
game, inside talk to the Moogle inside and he will tell you not to scare him 
like that, the party as you can expect is surprised to hear that the moogle 
can talk.

  "Human-loving, fast-talking, street-smart, SLAM-dancing...Moogle..."

Here you will be given the chance to name him, so go ahead and name him Mog. 
Here it appears that the "old psycho, Ramuh" came to him in his dreams and 
said to be expecting the party. And now he is going to join your party and he 
mentions something about Yeti muscle, he says he is here somewhere in the 
mines and if they can find him Mog will order him to join the party. Now 
check the wall DIRECTLY behind moogle to recieve a MOOGLE CHARM. 

Now head towards the northern mines and along the way you will see a blue 
dragon walking around, approach it to initiate a fight, if you are strong 
enough. Check the 8 dragons section at the top of the Side Areas portion of 
the FF6 walkthrough on how to beat it.  If you do decide to fight it, there 
is a save point just above, its in the exact same position as you saw it when
Kefka tried to raid Narche for the esper. Then continue on and you will see 
the esper you protected earlier, it will attack you.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
BOSS BATTLE: Tritoch       HP: 30,000
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
In this battle use any one of your strong magic attacks. Don't use any
elemental based attack or else you will heal him. Use your Blitz attacks
SwdTech Rage, etc. Keep your HP above 1000 to survive his Ice 3 attack. He 
will occasionally use Rasp which will drain away a porion of your MP, but 
make sure to keep your MPs in check.

After the battle you will have freed him from the prison of ice and he still 
can't believe that the war has lasted over a thousand years(it really hasn't 
since he was in ice for so long) and he will then lend you his power. Then 
afterwards an opening in the cliff will open up and go towards it and jump 
in. Then head for the left side and drop to the floor below and pick up the 
GUANTLET and go back to the upper floor and to the left is a treasure chest 
containing an X-ETHER, then take the MIDDLE staircase and then in this 
room(the one in which you started in) take the left but avoid the pitfalls as 
you can clearly see by the shading on the floor. 

Then go towards the treasure chest and you will be attacked by three Pugs, 
and this battle is pretty tough. They will use Pearl in this battle so keep
your HP above 800, but they will use Pearl as a counter attack against your 
Ultima attack. After the battle they will give you a MINERVA. Then go back to 
the room to the right and take the path all the way to the right and here you 
will drop to the bottom floor. Here make your way to the top room through the 
wooden bridge. Here in this room you will see a switch, ignore that switch 
and go to the right and hit that switch and you will fall to the room below. 
Here in this room DO NOT HEAD FOR THE DOOR JUST YET! Check the skull in the 
middle of the room and take the magicite Terrato out of the eye and then a 
monster will approach you and attack you.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
BOSS BATTLE: Yeti       HP: 17,200
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
This battle will be pretty easy, his physical attacks do pitiful damage. Use 
your most powerful magics in this battle and keep your HP up above 150 HP to 
survive its Blizzard attack, yes he is that weak.

After the battle have Mog talk to the Yeti monster and Mog will order him to 
join the party, and he does.

  "Admirer of bone-carvings, as strong as a gigas, a yeti pal with muscle!"

Here you will be given the chance to name him, just name him Umaro and be on 
with it. After the battle he will either join your current party or if your 
current party is full he will leave for the "big airship." Congratulations! 
You have now acquired a ton of new items and you have some new allies!

=============================================================================
MAGIC TOWER AND KEFKA'S TREASURE
Items: Safety Bit, Gem Box, Air Anchor, Stunner, Genji Shield, Force Armor
Party: Whomever
Recommended level: 50
=============================================================================

  NOTE: In this tower you can only use magic, your fight command WILL NOT
        show up on your command screen. Gogo however can use his fight
        command if you give him the fight command. Also monsters in here
        can be destroyed without knocking away their HP, if you use Osmose
        on some of these monsters they will die out as well.

Head for the Magic Tower, the place where you acquired Strago in. Here head
for the top of the tower. Its pretty linear, but its VERY long, like the
Pheonix Tower in FF5, except its not that long. In the first part of the 
tower and there is a door leading to a treasure chest, inside is a SAFETY BIT 
relic, go to the right of the treasure chest and check the wall and you will 
hear a noise, go outside and a door below you will open and enter it and pick 
up the AIR ANCHOR for Edgar. 

In the next part of the tower is another room leading to a GENJI SHLD, pick 
that up and continue onto the third part of the tower. In the third part of 
the tower is a STUNNER as well as a dragon, check the 8 Dragons portion of 
the Side Area section on how to defeat it. After picking that up go towards 
the fourth part of the tower and pick up the FORCE ARMOR. Then continue to 
the top of the tower and pick up the GEM BOX, then leave, but as you do a 
slew of ghosts will stop you and tell you to put back Kefka's treasure, but 
you can't since its too late. Then the MagiMaster will make his way around 
and attack you.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
BOSS BATTLE: MagiMaster      HP: 50,000
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

NOTE: In this battle you can Berserk him, his physical attacks are weak and
      he won't cast Ultima at the end because he's in Berserk mode. However
      if you do not have the magic Berserk, then follow the battle plan 
      below.

This boss is one tough customer. Immediately cast Life 3 on as many party
members as you can in this battle prior to beating him and keep your HP at a 
constant Max. Use all your strong magics like Meteor, Ultima, Flare, or 
Pearl. He is immensely powerful, his Fire 2 attack does about 1000 HP of 
damage, yes a weak spell like that does massive damage. Keep repeating the 
pattern and when you defeat him he will use Ultima, which will cause at LEAST 
5500 HP to every character, and if one character is standing it will do 9999 
HP of damage, but since Life 3 was cast prior to him using Ultima your 
character will come back to life.

After the battle the GEM BOX relic is now yours which lets you cast two
consecutive magics in one round.

=============================================================================
CYAN'S NIGHTMARE
Items: Remedy, Ice Shield, X-Potion, Flame Shield, Genji Glove, Beads, Ether,
       Elixir, Phoenix Down, Lump Of Metal
Party: Cyan and whomever
Recommended level: 38
=============================================================================

Remember Doma Castle? Head back there which is on the small island west of
the Veldt and make sure you have Cyan in your party. Earlier in the World of 
Balance this place was overrun with imperial troops, but after the incident 
most of the imperial troops were caught in the aftermath of the day of Kefka. 
Inside here there is an ETHER, and take the room to the right and sleep, but 
Cyan however is still asleep. Then three kids come in and introduce 
themselves being Curley, Larry, and Moe(what a coincidence). 

They are the three dream stooges and they want Cyan's soul and they all jump 
in Cyan's head as does the party. Here you will start off with your party
members divided, now you will have to find the others. Here take the left and 
then take the right door, and you will find your other party member 
unconsious, but one of the dream stooges walks off until he can reunite with 
his other borhters. Check with your party member to see if he or she is 
alright and then head to the door on the right. 

In here take the door on the top, now take the door on the right and your 
other party member is unconsious, but the other dream stooge runs off. Check 
your party member and then head to the left door. Here take the left side and 
enter that door. In here walk to the door and go inside, but before you can 
do that the three dream stooges bump you off.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
BOSS FIGHT: Curly, Larry, Moe     HP: 15,000(C) 10,000(L) 12,500(M)
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
As you cna expect in this battle use your best magic attacks. Use your Blitz, 
Rage, Tools, etc. Keep your HP up above 400 at all times unless you have 
something that can absorb lightnign or fire. I suggest keeping your magic 
spread in this battle, don't try to concentrate your attacks on one dream 
stooge otherwise if they recover they will immediately pull off their Delta 
Attack, which will stone a character(as seen in FFIV and FFV). They can 
revive as many times as needed to defeat you, but if you keep casting Ultima 
or Meteo they should go down one after the other.

After the battle go through the door and you will find a familiar place.
Its the Ghost Train, keep going towards the left and you will see Cyan being 
chased by a ghost, follow him inside. There is a treasure chest that can be 
accessed by pulling the switch near the door, you must go around and pick it 
up, but do it quickly otherwise you will not be able to reach it because the 
box will go back to its position if you are too slow, so having the SPRINT 
SHOES relic really helps here. Pick up the GENJI GLOVE and then go to the far 
left of this box car and pick up the lump of metal, after doing that put it 
in the treasure chest that would block your path each time you tried to reach 
for the treasure chest. Pick up the FLAME SHLD and then hit the switch to the 
left:

       A A B        A= Opened treasure chest
       B B A        B= Closed treasure chest

Memorize these positions as it saids so on the open book on the desk as it 
may save you. Then continue onto the left side to the next box car. Here in 
this box car hit the first switch and pick up the ICE SHLD and then hit the 
other switch to the left. Now go back to the first switch and hit the switch 
which will move the couch back to its regular position and it will clear the 
way for you to hit the middle switch. Hit the middle switch and then hit the 
first switch to the right. Then after that hit the last switch to the left 
and the two boxes will move out of the way and you can go under and to the 
other side. Here its the same set up with the treasure chests again, did you 
remember the pattern? Then do the exact same pattern that you saw earlier and 
then hit the switch and the left side's wall will open up. 

Now continue onto the next box car and inside is a save point so save your 
game and heal your wounds and continue onto the engine room to the left. In 
here there are three switches at the top right side, reverse the switches and 
then head out and this time you will be in magitek armor. Make your way 
outside and then go back inside, you heard me. If you continue to the right 
you will just continue to go around in circles. In here make your way around 
and outside you will see Cyan, he will run pass the bridge, as you follow him 
the bridge below will break and send you down below. You will now awaken in 
the room you rested in but you are still in Cyan's dream. 

Then Owain and Elayne will tell you to save Cyan, they tell you that you are 
inside Cyan's soul. Cyan continues to torture himself because he failed to 
defend Doma, the world is slowly dying, and then there's his family. A beast 
known as Wrexsoul is taking advantage of this situation, he is a monster made 
up of wretched souls made up or spirits from meaningless wars. Now a save 
point will pop up, so save your game and heal your wounds if any and then 
make your way to the center of the castle and you will see Cyan unconsious 
and Wrexsoul has already begun his dirty work, but its not too late.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
BOSS BATTLE: Wrexsoul & SoulSaver      HP: Wrexsoul(23,066) Soul Saver(3,066)
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

NOTE: When Wrexsoul is on the screen, cast X-Zone and he should be gone.
      Here in this battle he tells you that he will come back when you are 
      about to expire. THIS IS A CLUE! He then leaves. Don't bother with the 
      SoulSavers because you cannot destroy them because no matter HOW MANY 
      times you kill them they will come back to life. First aim your attacks 
      at your party members and knock out everybody except one. After that he 
      will come back and now strike him with everything you've got and revive 
      your party members and blast back for Cyan's sake. If he disappears do 
      the whole process again except you will have to have the party member 
      that was alive, when Wrexsoul came back, kill him or her and have a new 
      party member standing when Wrexsoul comes back. After the battle you 
      will recieve the POD BRACELET.

After the battle Cyan thanks you and he heard his wife and child calling to 
him and they gave him the courage to fight his own suffering. Then Owain and 
Elayne comes in, but Cyan feels that he is a man with no honor, but his 
family doesn't believe so. After the battle they say their last goodbyes for 
now and a sword appears, Cyan reaches for it and the party is now out of his 
nightmare. After the nightmare Cyan realizes that he has to forget about the 
past nad clears his soul of all doubt and confusion.

Then his swordsmanship level attain its peak level of skill meaning that you 
will now have full access to all his SwdTech abilities! Just try the Quadra 
Slice on level 7 and you'll be amazed! Now head back to the throne room in 
which you saw the magicite sitting on the chair and pick it up to recieve the 
magicite ALEXANDR. Now that you have ALEXANDR and all of Cyan's SwdTech 
abilties you'll be unstoppable!

STRAGO'S UNRELIEVING PAST
Items: Coral
Party: Relm, Strago, and whomever
Recommended level: 42
=============================================================================

Now head for Thamasa on the bottom right corner of the world map and inside
talk a scenario will automatically take place in here. NOTE: You must have
Strago and Relm in your party to comeplete this side-quest. Here inside Relm 
is pretty excited to be back home as Strago is just as excited as its time to 
relax, "home sweet home." Then Relm tells Strago that Gungho is hurt, the two 
go to check on him and it appears that Hidon, a beast that Strago and Gungho 
used to hunt, was the one responsible. He seems badly hurt and tells Strago 
to avenge him, but Strago hesistates.

It was no sweat when he was younger, but at his age its a lot more than he
had bargained for but he finally agrees and decides to avenge Gungho. Then
Relm wants to come along, but Strago spent to many years hunting for it and 
it's his obsession not Relm's. Relm wants to go but as its name implies the 
Hidon is extremely difficult to find, unless he goes alone it will not show 
itself. Relm then stays behind but decides to follow him anyways. Now that 
Strago and Relm have left your party, head towards Ebot's Rock up north and a 
opening inside will open up. Follow them inside but do not add any additional 
party members to your group. 

In here its clear tunnel vision from here on end, walk straight up and hit 
the switch and you will be transported to the next area. In here there is a 
treasure chest, talk to it and it will not let you pass unless you feed it 
some coral, but where can you find any? Now head down to the switch and in 
this room there is a save point up top so if you want you can save your game, 
but you really didn't do much. Now head towards the bottom switch and in this 
next room there is a treasure chest to the left which contains 3 pieces of 
CORAL. 

Then continue onto the left and step on the switch to the next area and you 
will be back at the area where the treasure chest would not let you through. 
But now that you have some Coral feed it to him and he will eat it, but he 
still wants more. So head back to the bottom switch and you should be near 
the entrance, step on the switch again and to the right is another treasure 
chest containing a piece of CORAL, then head for the switch at the bottom. In
this room head for the bottom left and pick up 2 pieces of CORAL and then 
head for the switch directly to the right. In this room check the treasure 
chest for 3 pieces of CORAL and then head all the way to the right for 
another 3 pieces of CORAL and then step on the switch to the right. 

Now in this room save your game and heal your wounds if any and then head for
the switch to the next room. Here in this room head for the top and pick up 
three pieces of CORAL and then head for the switch to the right of that and 
here in this room pick up 5 pieces of CORAL to the left and then head for the 
top switch and you will be back at the treasure chest that wanted some more 
CORAL. Feed your new stash, but he's so greedy and still wants some more. So 
head down to the switch and in this room there is a treausure chest to the 
left to pick up a piece of CORAL and then head up to the next switch. 

Here in this room step on the switch leading to the next room and in here 
check the bottom for 2 pieces of CORAL and then head for the top left switch. 
In this room pick up 5 pieces of CORAL to the right and then step on the 
switch to the next room. Here there is 2 pieces of CORAL to the left, then 
head further left and onto the next switch. In this room there is another 
treasure chest to the left containing 3 pieces of CORAL, then make your way 
to the left and step on that switch. In this next room to the left is 3 
pieces of CORAL, after that step on the switch leading to the next room. Here 
in this room to the left is 3 pieces of CORAL, then head for the right side 
and step on the switch. 

Here there is a switch to the right of you, GO AROUND it and to the top to 
pick up 3 pieces of CORAL and then head for the switch to the left. In this 
next room head straight up and pick up 2 pieces of CORAL and to the bottom 
right of this room pick up 3 pieces of CORAL and then hit the switch to the 
right and you should be at the entrance of Ebot's Rock. Step on it again and
you will be at the entrance again, but step on the switch up top and onto the 
next room. Here there is a save point at the top, so definitely save your 
game and heal your wounds if any and continue onto the next room via the 
switch at the bottom. 

You will be at the same room again, so hit the switch at the bottom again, 
you will be at the same save room again so hit the switch once more. Here in 
this room head down below to pick up a piece of CORAL and then step on the 
switch to the left of it and in this next room which looks the same as the 
last one, head down below and pick up 5 pieces of CORAL and then step on the 
switch to the left of the tresure chest. Here is another save point, so save 
your game if you want and heal your wounds if you want and then continue on. 
There is another save point in this room, but ignore it and continue on. 

In this room check the treasure chest to the left and pick up a piece of 
CORAL and then head to the bottom left of this room and step on the switch to 
the next room. You will now be in the room with the coral eating treasure 
chest, feed him your next stash and he will be completely full. He hesistates 
for a while and gives out his odor, the party then gets agitated and reminds 
him symbolically that they want to get through. So he does, then walk up the 
middle and and talk to it to initiate a fight.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
BOSS BATTLE: Hidon & Hidonite(4)      HP: 25,000(Hidon) 3,000(Hidonite)
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
In this battle its best that you spread your magic. Your first priority is to 
get the Hidonites and then attack Hidon, so any strong spread magic will 
do(ala Ultima). Once they are out of the way Hidon will use his GrandTrain 
attack, it does massive damage so its good to keep your HP above 1100 just to 
be safe. He will use Poison, so cure it once he does. After the battle you 
will recieve a WARP STONE. NOTE: If Hidon uses his GrandTrain attack on 
Strago that means Strago will learn it after the battle. Note that it is his 
STRONGEST Lore attack and its quite powerful.

NOTE: If you do not get the GrandTrain Lore Magic, you can re-visit this
      place again and fight him again, however its a pain to go through
      Ebot's Rock again, but its WELL worth it!

Here after the battle Strago is excited that he has beaten Hidon, he then 
tells Gungho that he is avenged. He then tells the good news to Gungho and 
Gungho is shocked. Gungho then gets all cheery and jittery and Strago asks 
how are his wounds healing, and Gungho says their fine. Then that evening 
Strago and Gungho are talking over it in the middle of the night. He stared 
Hidon in the middle of the eyes, lifted his staff, and let him have it! 
Strago wanted to show his enemy the true meaning of the word "hero." Then 
Gungho walks outside and talks to Relm, Gungho tells her that he's off and 
talks about his wounds. 

But before he can talk Relm wants to thank him, Gungho gave Strago a reason 
that has tormented Strago for decades, even if he was faking Hidon meant 
business. Gungho is equally amazed at the granddaughter Strago raised as he 
is at the defeat of Hidon by Strago. But Relm reminds him of his terrible
acting, only Strago could have been taken in by such an awful performance! 
Gungho gets agitated as Relm runs inside the house. Now you have successfully 
defeat Hidon and hopefully you did learn GRANDTRAIN, if not then I have one 
word for you: "Gameshark"

THE LOST CASTLE AND THE REIGN OF ODIN
Items: Ether, X-Ether, Wing Edge, Gold Hairpin, Punisher, Offering, Magicite,
       Blizzard Orb, Trump
Party: Whomever
Recommended level: 40
=============================================================================

Remember where you had last left Figaro Castle? Right on the top most eastern 
continent on the desert. Return there and tell the driver that you want to go 
to Figaro. During the middle of your voyage the driver notices something odd 
about the stratum, he will ask you if you want to start again or stop. Choose 
stop and head for the basement where the jailors were previously kept. In 
here to the far right the door has opened up, so go inside and in this room 
and pick up an ETHER and another WING EDGE for Locke then head to the right 
door and check the treasure chest and a Master Pug will attack you.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
BOSS BATTLE: Master Pug    HP: 22,000    ITEM: Gradeus
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
This guy is TOUGH. Use your most powerful magics and Blitz, SwdTech, Lore,
etc. to defeat this guy. Keep your HP above 1500, he will counter attack with 
StepMine everytime you attack him which causes about near 1400 HP of damage, 
so you will need to heal after it, if your levels are too low then your gone, 
so bring that character back to life. Don't use any elemental attacks against 
it because it will absorb your attacks. Strago's GrandTrain Lore attack works 
here as he will not counter attack against it. He will constantly change 
barriers so unless you know exactly what he is weak against, then avoid using 
elemental attacks. NOTE: Strago here can learn Step Mine from Master Pug, it 
does not have to connect on him either!

Now afterwards head for either door to the left, along the way make sure you 
pick up the TRUMP for Setzer and then continue onto the left. In this next 
room to the left is an X-POTION and to the bottom is a MAGICITE. After that 
take the stairs down and in here there is a save point, so save your game and 
heal your wounds if any then continue onto the left. The party then notices a 
gaint castle and a scenario of a portion of the War of the Magi takes place. 
The guards are immediately taken out as an esper shows them its magic, but 
another guard wants to show them his esper magic.

It was a thousand years in the past that a battle was waged here, the guards 
ask if Odin's wounds are healed, but it appears that the guards are fresh out 
of options so they will leave the battle in Odin's hands. Odin then shows the 
espers his Atom Edge in which gets them all, then another esper comes by as 
Odin tries his Atom Edge, it doesn't work. The esper then turns Odin into 
stone, but Odin tells him not to turn him into a magicite, so the esper 
doesn't. The legend tells of a great battle between Odin and a powerful 
sorcerer. Now continue on and enter the left side of the castle and check the 
treasure chest and a KatanaSoul will attack you.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
BOSS BATTLE: KatanaSoul       HP: 37,620    ITEM: Offering
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
Here in this battle its pretty straight forward, attack him with every one of 
your strong magic attacks. Watch for his Imperial Dart attack, it will kill 
you even if you are at 9999 HP. He will also use GP Rain and that will take 
off massive damage as well, keep your HP at max if possible and keep on 
attacking. Watch for his Ashura Dart attack which causes near 8300 HP of 
damage, so you can't do much about that, basically keep your HP up and 
attack.

After the battle go to the inside of the castle and to the throne room and
touch the Odin statue, it will turn into a Magicite Shard. Now continue to 
the top right and into the room and pick up a GOLD HAIRPIN and a BLIZZARD
ORB, and they are both relics. Now go to the right and down the stairs check 
the sparkling orb, it tells that the queen is in love with Odin and it breaks 
every single rule in her society. If Terra is in your party she will realize 
the love between an esper and a human. Now check the right pot in the room to 
pick up an X-ETHER. Now return to the middle of the throne room and go one 
step down from where Odin was standing and hit the "A" button on the SNES 
version or hit the "X" button on the PSX version and a switch will open up. 

Return to the room where you read the Queen's diary and a staircase will now 
open up go down the ascending staircase and there is a blue dragon in here, 
if you think your strong enough to fight it then do so, check my guide above 
if you have trouble defeating it. Afterwards go to the center statue in this 
room and you will see that the queen has been turned to stone, then a tear 
comes from the statue as Odin gains to the next level and becomes Raiden. 
Don't worry if you didn't learn METEOR from Odin, if you've defeated all the 
dragons you will get Crusader and learn METEOR 10 times as fast. Afterwards 
you will now have the esper Raiden in your hands!

THE DEMON THAT ROAMS THE AIR
Items: Bahamut Magicite
Party: Whomever
Recommended level: 32
=============================================================================

In the World of Ruin, on your airship fly around the World of Ruin, fly 
around the world and eventually a DoomGlaze will attack you.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
BOSS BATTLE: DoomGlaze     HP: 55,555
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
This battle shouldn't be too hard. Keep attacking him until he's gone. He 
will leave after you lose him about 8,000 HP. NOTE: You can defeat him 
quickly like you can with most bosses by first casting Vanish on him and then 
X-Zone. Its a qucik victory yes, but you will not get the BAHAMUT esper.

After the battle keep roaming around the world and the DoomGlaze will 
approach you again. Keep doing this five times and he will drop a BAHAMUT 
esper. Congratulations! You have now recived the strongest esper in the game, 
too bad Leviathan was never in this game!

=============================================================================

                              ------------------
                              Esper Magic System
                              ------------------

  Final Fantasy VI introduces a new system which has been dubbed the "Esper
  System" in which previous Final Fantasy games you had to buy magic(Final
  Fantasy) or earn them by levels(Final Fantasy IV). However the Esper system
  does neither instead as you find and search for espers, they turn into
  magicite and you will inherit all the magics the esper has to offer just
  as long as you fight in battle with them. At the end of each battle you
  will earn Magic Points, and no they are not your MP. Instead consider them
  as something like Ability Points if you may. Okay, lets say you have Raiden
  and Meteor is at 10%, that means when you earn 1 magic point, you will
  earn 10 magic points, so its basically a bit of multiplying. When you reach
  100% for that certain magic you will have already learned that magic.
  Some magics take very little battles to learn or they may take a lot, it
  all depends. Also everybody learns the magic at the same rate, with a few
  exceptions. Sometimes you don't even need a magicite to learn magic, for
  example if you have the PALADIN shield equipped during battle, you can
  learn Ultima, your progress can be seen on the magic listing menu. Terra
  and Celes can learn magic on their own but it takes a very long time to
  learn them all. Also you can learn up to six different magics at a time
  or as many as the esper has because you will earn magic points for all the
  magics that are on the esper. Once each character has learned at least
  one magic spell, a Magic command will automatically pop up on the battle
  screen. Below here are a list of different magic spells that can be learned
  and a brief description of each and also the espers and the magics that
  you can learn from them.


  NOTE: When you recieve a Magicite as an item, it does not mean that its
        a new esper, its actually a random summon to be used in battle. And
        as you can expect there are relics that decrease the amount of MP
        used during battle like the Economizer or Gold Hairpin.
