-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
                                  ======
----------------------------------Magics-------------------------------------
                                  ======
--------------
Cure     MP: 5
--------------
  Weak healing magic. Strong against undead. Heals about 70-2000 of any loss
  HP.

--------------
Cure 2  MP: 25
--------------
  Medium healing magic. Stronger against undead. Heals about 350-5000 of any
  loss HP.

--------------
Cure 3  MP: 40
--------------
  High healing magic. Strongest against undead. Heals about 800-9500 of any
  loss HP.

--------------
Life    MP: 30
--------------
  Recovers any party member that is in the swoon status, can be used against
  undead, but not all. Recovers swoon party member to 12% of max HP.

--------------
Life 2  MP: 60
--------------
  Recovers any party member that is in the swoon status, can e used against
  undead, but not all. Recovers swoon party member to maximum HP.

--------------
Antdot   MP: 3
--------------
  Recovers any poison or bio status the party member may have.

--------------
Remedy  MP: 15
--------------
  Recovers all abnormal ailments including Confusion, Stop, Poison, Bio, 
  Sleep, Blind, Berserk, Stone, and Charm. It does not cure however Frozen,
  Imp, or Zombie status.

--------------
Regen   MP: 10
--------------
  When casted the party member's HP gradually refills after few rounds or
  so.

--------------
Life 3  MP: 50
--------------
  When casted the party member who becomes swooned will recover back to
  health with 12% of maximum HP.

--------------
Fire     MP: 4
--------------
  Weak fire attack. Works well against undead and ice based monsters. This
  can be used to heal party members that are wearing fire based shields and
  armors. 

--------------
Ice      MP: 5
--------------
  Weak ice attack. Works well against fired based monsters or anybody with
  an ice weakness. This can be used to heal party members that are wearing
  ice based shields and armors.

--------------
Bolt     MP: 6
--------------
  Weak lightning attack. Works well against water based monsters and sea
  creatures. This can be used to heal party members that are wearing 
  lightning based shields and armors.

--------------
Poison   MP: 3
--------------
  Poison based attack. Once connected a gradual drop in HP every few rounds.
  Can be used against oppostion or party member.

--------------
Drain   MP: 15
--------------
  Drains opponent's HP and replenishes caster. Depending on how much HP you
  have determines how much you will absorb. If you are in desperate need of 
  HP then you will absorb more HP or if your HP is high you will absorb very
  little HP. Avoid using this on Lamia based monsters as well as undead
  monsters.

--------------
Fire 2  MP: 20
--------------
  Medium fire based attack. Works well against undead monsters and ice based
  monsters or any opposition weak against fire. This can be used to heal any
  party wearing fired based shields and armors. Can be used against the 
  opposition or party members.

--------------
Ice2    MP: 21
--------------
  Medium ice based attack. Works well against fire based monsters. This can 
  be used to heal any party member wearing fire based shields and armors. Can 
  be used against the opposition or party member.

--------------
Bolt 2  MP: 22
--------------
  Medium lightning based attack. Works well against water based monsters or
  sea creatures. This can be used to heal any party member wearing lightning
  based shields and armors. Can be used against the opposition or party 
  members.

--------------
Bio     MP: 26
--------------
  Poison elemental based attack. Once cast the opposition or party member
  will suffer servere damage at first and a rapid and gradual drop in HP
  will follow.

--------------
Fire 3  MP: 51
--------------
  Strongest fire based attack. Works well against undead monsters and ice
  based enemies. This will heal any party member wearing fire based shields
  and armor. Can be used against the opposition or party member.

--------------
Ice 3   MP: 52
--------------
  Strongest ice based attack. Works well against fire based monsters or any
  fire based enemies. This will heal any party member wearing fire based
  shields and armor. Can be used against the opposition or party member.

--------------
Bolt 3  MP: 53
--------------
  Stronest lightning based attack. Works well against water based monsters or
  sea creatures. This will heal any party member wearing fire based shields 
  and armors. Can be used against the opposition or party member.

--------------
Break   MP: 25
--------------
  An attack that will stone any opposition or party member, however this will
  not work anybody immune to the stone affect. This will instantly kill the
  opposition, but an affected party member can be cured with a Remedy or 
  Soft.

--------------
Doom    MP: 35
--------------
  Once casted against the opposition or party member instant death is
  dealt upon that target. This will not work against anybody immune to it
  like most bosses.

--------------
Pearl   MP: 40
--------------
  This is another name for Holy. This is a pearl-elemental attack or holy
  elemental attack. This works well against the undead and can be used
  against the opposition or party member.

--------------
Flare   MP: 45
--------------
  Despite its name, this is not a fire attack. This is a rather powerful
  attack that causes massive damage to one target. This can be used against
  the opposition or party member.

--------------
Demi    MP: 33
--------------
  An attack that reduces the opposition or party member's current HP to
  half. This will not work against anybody immune to it like most bosses
  obviously.

--------------
Quartr  MP: 48
--------------
  A more powerful version of Demi. This will reduce any opposition or 
  party member's current HP to 25%. This will not work against anybody
  immune to it like most bosses obviously.

--------------
X-Zone  MP: 53
--------------
  Summons a giant rift in space to open up and swallow the opposition.
  Works best on anybody that is vanished.

--------------
Meteor  MP: 62
--------------
  Somewhat weakened from previous Final Fantasy games. A giant black
  hole opens up and sends herds of meteorites towards the opposition.
  This will hit the opposition on both sides even in a pincer attack, but
  its not concentrated. However this cannot be reflected by a Wall.

--------------
Ultima  MP: 80
--------------
  The strongest of all magics. Immense magical energy erupts around
  a giant aqua colored sphere hitting all enemies on screen even in a
  pincer attack. Becomes half effective if spread among two or more targets.
  No barrier or Wall can protect against its power.

--------------
Quake   MP: 50
--------------
  A super powerful Earthquake attack that's so strong it even affects the
  entire party. Use float to avoid damage when cast. This is an 
  unconcentrated attack and cannot be reflected by a Wall.

--------------
W Wind  MP: 75
--------------
  An unconcentrated near fatal attack that will leave opposition or
  party member with a few drops of HP. Anybdoy can be affected by this
  friend, foe, or caster at random.

--------------
Merton  MP: 80
--------------
  Powerful piercing fire attack that attacks both party members and the
  opposition. A Fire4 attack hits everybody and the caster will absorb the
  loss HP. However any party member wearing a fire based shield or armor
  can absorb the fire attack.

--------------
Scan     MP: 3
--------------
  This magic will allow you to view your opponent's HP and any weaknesses
  that they may have. Should work 98% of the time.

--------------
Slow     MP: 5
--------------
  This magic will slow either the opposition or a party member's wait guage
  so that there is less attacks or commands being inputted during battle.
  Very disadvantageous and can be cured with Dispel or Fast.

--------------
Rasp    MP: 12
--------------
  A magic effecting attack that takes away either the opposition's HP or
  your party members' but you cannot absorb the loss HP.

--------------
Mute     MP: 8
--------------
  This magic silences either the opposition or a party member which disallows
  them to use magic. Use a REMEDY or the Remedy spell to cure.

--------------
Safe    MP: 12
--------------
  This magic will put a Safe protectant seal around the party member which
  protects against physical attacks making all physical attacks half
  effective from normal effectiveness. Can be taken down with Dispel.

--------------
Sleep    MP: 5
--------------
  This will put either the opposition to sleep or a party member to sleep.
  This can be cured by either hitting your party member or the opposition.

--------------
Muddle   MP: 8
--------------
  This magic will make either the opposition or a party member go into a
  confusion status, attack your party member to be cured or use a REMEDY
  or Remedy spell.

--------------
Haste   MP: 10
--------------
  This magic will make either the opposition or party member's wait guage
  go faster allowing for more attacks in a SLIGHTLY shorter amount of time.
  IF you are dumb enough to cure this, use Slow.

--------------
Stop    MP: 10
--------------
  This magic causes either the opposition or your party member to become
  paralyzed making them uneffective during battle. This can only be cured
  with the Dispel spell or if you wait until your character snaps out of it.

--------------
Berserk MP: 16
--------------
  This magic will make either the opposition or your party member go
  berserk, unable to control themselves they will go into a fury that causes
  critical hits the majority of the times and the wait guage is always full.
  Becareful on using it on a party member, they cannot use items or magic
  when they are in this status.

--------------
Float   MP: 17
--------------
  This magic will cause the party members to float, thus allowing you to
  avoid damage floors like magma and lets you avoid Quake attacks during
  battle. Can be spread among party members.

--------------
Imp     MP: 10
--------------
  This magic can be used against either the opposition or a party member
  as it will turn the target into an Imp causing the defense and attack
  power to drop. This can be used even if you are on Mute status and can
  be used to cure Imp status on an effected party member. NOTE: On the
  Dinosaur forest you can defeat the dinosaurs for Imp weapons, which are
  rather effective in Imp status.

--------------
Rflect  MP: 22
--------------
  This magic can be used either against the opposition or a party member and
  it will reflect any magic spell(except for W Wind, Merton, Meteor, Ultima,
  Quake, X-Zone, and Dispel) for a certain amount of rounds. If an opponent
  has a Wall set up, you can reflect your won magic off of your party member
  to damage the opposition.

--------------
Shell   MP: 15
--------------
  This magic will put up a protective barrier that cuts all magic attacks
  down in half with the exception of Ultima, Meteor, and W Wind. Can be
  taken down with Dispel.

--------------
Vanish  MP: 18
--------------
  This magic will make the opposition or party member vanish, causing hits
  to be less successfully effective. Cast this first and then X-Zone, and
  watch the majority of your opponents go off, even against most bosses!

--------------
Haste2  MP: 38
--------------
  This magic is like Haste except it will cast Haste to every member in your
  party or the oppositon allowing for less time between attacks to be 
  consumed. Can be disinfected with Dispel.

--------------
Slow 2  MP: 26
--------------
  This magic is like Slow except it will cast Slow to every party member in
  your party or the opposition allowing for more time between attacks to
  be consumed. Can be disinfected with Dispel.

--------------
Osmose   MP: 1
--------------
  This magic will allow you to absorb magic points from the opposition, 
  the more you need the more you absorb and the less you need the less you
  will absorb. One of the more useful spells in the game.

--------------
Warp    MP: 20
--------------
  This will allow the party member to escape a dungeon or used to escape
  from battle. Use this to get out of Kefka's Tower if you don't know how.

--------------
Quick   MP: 99
--------------
  This magic will allow for double commands to be executed while being
  completely uninterrupted. Very powerful.

--------------
Dispel  MP: 25
--------------
  This magic cannot be reflected as it will remove any spell effect from
  the opposition or party member. Even if the magic effects are layered
  one cast can remove all. You can only remove Safe, Shell, Wall, Haste,
  and Slow.

=============================================================================
=============================================================================

             ---------------------------------------------------
             Final Fantasy Collection/Anthology Omake/Bonus Mode
             ---------------------------------------------------

  Okay, so the Omake mode is only open to Final Fantasy VI, but here is a
  short list of what can be acquired once you beat the game on Final Fantasy
  VI.

      ????=Not available at the beginning of the game, you must beat the game
           to unlock it.

------
Studio
------
   
   =======
   Theater
   =======

     ++++++++++++++++++
     The Magitek Empire
     ++++++++++++++++++
     The FMV intro for the game, elapsed time: 3:16:42

     +++++++++++++++++
     For the lovers...(????)
     +++++++++++++++++
     The FMV ending for the game, elapsed time: 3:32:00

     +++++
     PILOT(????)
     +++++
     The promotional television ad displayed in Japan. Elapsed time: 2:03:52
     NOTE: This only contains a few scenes not in the ending or intro of the
           game like when the show a close up of one of the IAF ships being
           blown up by Setzer's Gambit style Full House!


   =======
   Gallery
   =======

    NOTE: In the Gallery, each time you view a picture you can hit the
          "triangle" button to zoom in on the picture, press it again to
          see the normal view. You can also use your directional pad to
          scroll up and down on the various artworks.

     +++++++++++++
     Art Gallery 1
     +++++++++++++
     The art gallery shows the drawings and planning for the Intro FMV.

     +++++++++++++
     Art Gallery 2
     +++++++++++++
     More pictures and art of the FMV intro, but rough sketches are shown.

     +++++++++++++++++++
     Art Gallery 3(????)
     +++++++++++++++++++
     A lot more pictures and art, but this time its from the FMV ending, the
     art gallery seems to be dedicated to Celes. Also contains some 
     additional pictures of FMV shots not seen in the ending.

     +++++++++++++++++++
     Art Gallery 4(????)
     +++++++++++++++++++
     The drawing plan and boards for the FMV ending, as you can expect these
     are rough sketches, but the artists are clearly talented.

     +++++++++++++++++++
     Art Gallery 5(????)
     +++++++++++++++++++
     The gallery shows mainly the FMV still shots of the intro, and a lot of
     other rendered images of the 4 main characters(excluding Kururu) are 
     shown as well. Near the end a still shot of Rubicant is shown along with
     some rough sketches of pencil artwork for the art for FFIV. Also note
     that the esper Carbunkle(from FFV) is wearing some rather hip and cool
     sneakers.


------
Status
------

     Shows best and worst performances including number of steps, time and
     the amount of GP you finished off the game with. At the bottom are the
     percentages of your characters, all of the magics, HP, MP, levels, and
     status are calculated to give your character's temporary ending results.
     Play again to get the best time, but beware of the load time and slow
     down!


------
Secret
------

  ========
  Bestiary
  ========

       +++++++++++++++
       Pre-Catastrophe
       +++++++++++++++

       Listing of all monsters, including weaknesses, levels, HP, MP, and
       more. These are listings of the all monsters before the world of
       Ruin.

       ++++++++++++++++++++++
       Post-Catastrophe(????)
       ++++++++++++++++++++++

       Listing of all the monsters, including weaknesses, levels, HP, MP
       and more. These are listings of al the monsters after the World of
       Balance.

  ===============
  Esperiary(????)
  ===============
   
       These are listings of all espers found in the game, including brief
       description, magic learning list, and level up bonuses. Does not tell
       where to find the espers.

  ================
  Lore Magic(????)
  ================
      
       These are listings of the monsters in which Strago can learn new Lore
       attacks from, including brief description and MP used along with
       other monsters that can teach Strago new Lore attacks.

  ===============
  Colosseum(????)
  ===============

       A VERY detail breakdown of all the weapons, armor, relic, and items
       you can get if you win the battle against the listed enemy.



  Well that's it, sure the game offers Bonus Mode, but then there's the
  slowdown that you have to deal with, so its your choice, but for me it
  was worth it, even though the FF5 translation was a bit whack.

=============================================================================
=============================================================================

                          ---------------------
                          Colesseum Bet Listing
                          ---------------------

  This section was mainly provided by the Bonus section in FFVI, thanks a lot
  Square! On the world map northwestern part, you will find a castle of some
  sort that looks a lot like the Opera House. Inside you can bet your current
  items and place them against an opponent HOPEFULLY for a better prize.
  NOTE: If you bet items that you can buy, you will face off against Chupon,
        who will most likely use his Sneeze attack and blow you out of battle
        but you do not lose the item you placed bet on. 

=============================================================================

                               Best Times

  Final Fantasy VI:
  First Time Playing: 28:12
  Best Time Playing: 6:03
  Best Time playing through all(including Side Areas and all obtaining all
       magic spells and reaching level 99): 69:14


  NOTE: The clock in both the SNES and PSX versions are not accurate times
        and they are 50% slower, so you will need to double the actual
        hours in the game to get your actual total Real Time.
